Explanation of Patents by the Ministry of Industries 57

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industries' response to the inquiry from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce states: "The Chinese Patent Law has not yet been revised and promulgated, therefore foreign patented products have no patent rights under Chinese jurisdiction." Minister Chen explained that this instruction absolutely cannot be construed as granting Chinese merchants special rights to imitate foreign patented products. The Provisional Regulations for Encouraging Industrial Technology, promulgated on November 30, 1932, clearly stipulate in Article 1 that "Any citizen of the Republic of China who first invents an industrial product or method may apply for an award in accordance with these regulations." If it is found that the product or method has already been patented by others in China or abroad, or if interested parties raise objections or provide conclusive evidence, the Ministry will not grant a patent. If a registration has been obtained by mistake, it shall be revoked. This instruction is based on the Sino-American Commercial Treaty of 1903. Article 10 of that treaty clearly states that for inventions by American citizens, patent rights can only be recognized after China has established a patent law and a dedicated patent office, and approval has been obtained in accordance with the law. The issue of patent law is currently under investigation based on precedents from various countries, with the aim of establishing it soon so that the patent office can be established as soon as possible to comply with the treaty and allow foreign merchants to obtain patent rights in accordance with the law. Even before the patent law is formulated and promulgated, if domestic citizens apply for awards in accordance with the regulations of the Industrial Encouragement Law, and it is found that they are clearly imitating foreign patented products, or if interested parties raise objections, patents will not be granted. This implicitly contains the intention of protecting the patent rights of foreign merchants. (Special dispatch on the 25th)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industries' response to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's inquiry regarding whether foreign merchants have patents in China stated that the Chinese Patent Law has not yet been revised and promulgated, therefore foreign patented products have no patent rights under Chinese jurisdiction. A responsible person from the Ministry of Industries explained the instruction, stating that Chinese merchants cannot enjoy the special right to imitate foreign patented products as a result of this instruction. The Provisional Regulations for Encouraging Industrial Technology, promulgated last November, stipulate that citizens can apply for awards in accordance with the regulations, but if the applied-for product has already been patented by others in China or abroad, or if interested parties raise objections, the patent will be revoked. Furthermore, this instruction is based on Article 10 of the Sino-American Commercial Treaty of 1903, which stipulates that for inventions by American citizens, patents can only be granted after China has established a patent law and a dedicated patent office and obtained approval in accordance with the law. The Ministry of Industries is currently investigating precedents, formulating patent laws, and establishing a dedicated patent office as soon as possible so that foreign merchants can also obtain patent rights. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 25th)

Dentsu Tokyo, 25th: The public trial of Goto Eihan and others, defendants in the May 15 Incident on the army side, began after Prosecutor Hiyosaka read the facts of the prosecution. Goto Eihan was then questioned. Legal Officer Shimada examined the facts. Mr. Goto gave a routine statement of his family relations and experiences. The questions and answers between the legal officer and the defendant were as follows: (Q) When did you start the movement to reform the country? (A) In Showa 6, under the guidance of Lieutenant Kanbe, a senior officer, I began to participate in the movement to reform the country by studying the national polity with military personnel. As a result of the study, I realized that the current situation in Japan has many things related to the essence of the national polity, etc., citing the military's admonition to explain. (Q) What are your thoughts on the current society? (A) Political parties tend to pursue party strategies, becoming tools of plutocrats and financial cliques. Therefore, issues such as buying US dollars and military reductions are all like this. In the meantime, small and medium-sized industrialists and the proletariat are suffering from food shortages, so the ministers around the monarch are alienated from us citizens and those above. It is not to criticize American gold worship and communism. (Q) What is the reason for taking direct action? (A) At that time, the Tohoku region was experiencing famine, and the children of poor rural areas were incorporated into the army, and they had the feeling of pulling the hair behind their heads. Following them on expeditions, the financial cliques and politicians were only concerned with their own private interests. Mr. Goto continued, "Soldiers who love the country and are loyal will surely rise up one after another." He then stated his awareness of cooperation and compromise with comrades in the navy, saying that he heard that the navy wanted to cooperate, so he compromised, not because of the navy's request. Moreover, from the beginning, the comrades and others had made up their minds. He then spoke in detail about the planning of the incident. The court was adjourned at 2:30 PM.

We, who act in military uniforms, are acting in the name of the children of His Majesty the Emperor." At 11:30 AM, a break was announced. The court reopened at 1:00 PM. Lieutenant Koga continued, "In mid-May, during the special Diet session, we planned to attack the Diet. Tianjin Communists Reform 92

Wang Baozhong and Others Awaken and Return

There Are Only a Hundred or So Communists in Tianjin

Tianjin Special Dispatch: In recent years, the Yangtze River region has been plagued by the Communists, causing immense suffering. Communism is also beginning to sprout and grow in North China. However, the people of the North possess a robust character and deeply ingrained traditional moral values. Coupled with the strict enforcement of arrests by the police, the Communists find it difficult to operate freely. Only local labor strikes exhibit slight red undertones. Therefore, aside from ordinary workers who are easily tempted due to the hardships of life, it is the youth from middle schools and universities who feel frustrated due to their inability to find employment in society. Furthermore, with their weak willpower, they fall into the trap once lured. Earlier this month, the activities of the so-called "Tianjin Municipal Guidance Committee of the Chinese Communist Youth League" were discovered. The Tianjin Municipal Party Department of the Kuomintang, in conjunction with the Special Task Force of the Public Security Bureau, conducted a thorough investigation and lured Wu Peicang, the Standing Committee Member and Secretary of the League, from the concession area to Chinese territory and arrested him. Wu confessed that the organization's headquarters were located at a certain address on Jinyiwei Bridge. Police detectives were immediately dispatched to the location, where they captured Wang Baozhong, a member of the Standing Committee, and Zhang Lihua (female, original name Dong Qirong), a branch administrator. Subsequently, based on their confessions, they successively arrested Liu Yazhai, the secretary of the branch at the Higher Industrial School and secretary of the Anti-Imperialist branch; Liu Senlin, the acting secretary of the branch at the Higher Industrial School; Wu Tianmin, the secretary of the street branch; Zhang Zhenmin, the leader of the assault team (formerly of the puppet municipal committee); and League members Zhang Zongqian, Zhang Zongjian, Yang Yinshuo, Zhang Zhensheng, and more than ten others. They were detained in the preferential treatment room of the Public Security Bureau. Shao Hua, a member of the Standing Committee of the Municipal Party Department, interrogated them along with personnel from the Special Task Force. They all confessed to joining the Communist Party without denial. After careful examination, Shao and others found that these individuals were all young, and Wu Peicang and Wang Baozhong were university students with excellent qualifications. It would be regrettable to punish them by law for going astray due to a moment's weakness. Therefore, they explained the fallacies of the Communist Party's heresies and the crimes they had committed in deceiving the masses. They were told that if they could repent, they would be given a path to reform. At this point, they all confessed their innermost feelings, admitting that they had joined due to enticement, curiosity, or the bitterness of life. They had all joined the party around February of this year, and although it had only been half a year, they had gained a complete understanding of the Communist Party's inner workings and expressed their realization. Finally, they completely disclosed the Communist Party's organization and plans in North China. The Municipal Party Department reported this to the Central Government, which approved the issuance of a declaration of withdrawal from the party, pardoning their past actions and allowing them to reform. The Municipal Party Department then held a reception for the press at 3:00 PM on the 22nd, where Wang Baozhong, Wu Cangpei, and others successively reported on various inside stories of the Communist Party. According to Wang Baozhong, there are only about one hundred Communist Party members in Tianjin, mostly students, followed by workers, with very weak influence. It is feared that they will soon naturally dissolve. (July 23)

Shen Honglie Returns to Qingdao 93

Representatives from All Sectors Welcome Him at the Station

Shen States That He Will Still Resign to the Central Government

Jinan Dispatch: At 11:00 PM on the 23rd, a long-distance telephone call from Qingdao reported that Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie, due to the earnest retention by all parties and abandoning his resignation intentions, returned to Qingdao from Weihai by boat on the 21st with Qingdao representatives Song Yuting and others. They arrived in Yantai that day. They were originally scheduled to return to Qingdao via Weixian from Yantai on the 22nd, but because all sectors in Yantai held a welcome meeting, they stayed for a day. It was not until 8:00 AM this morning (the 23rd) that they departed Yantai with the Qingdao representatives, traveling south along the Yantai-Weixian road by car. Rong Guangxing, Brigade Commander of the Eighty-Seventh Brigade, Zhang Kuiwen, Director of the Public Security Bureau, and representatives from all sectors all went to the bus station to see them off. At noon, Shen and his party arrived in Weixian. Li Wenli, the Magistrate of Weixian County, and representatives of the garrison commander from all sectors all went to the station to welcome them. Shen briefly exchanged greetings with the welcomers, and then boarded two carriages of a reserved special train prepared by the Jiaoji Railway, which were attached to the Jiaoji Railway's sixth train, departing Weixian at 1:08 PM and arriving in Qingdao at 6:30 PM in the afternoon. Ge Guangting, Chairman of the Jiaoji Railway Committee, important party, government, and military figures, consuls from various countries, and representatives from all sectors also went to the station to welcome them. After Shen got off the train, he briefly interacted with the welcomers, then left the station on foot to Zhongshan Road, and then took a car back to his private residence for rest. Qingdao's all sectors, assuming that Shen still intends to resign, sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Premier Wang Jingwei, and Huang Fu and He Yingqin in Peiping today, to retain Shen, requesting them to send a telegram to Shen to dispel his resignation intentions. Also, after Shen arrived in Qingdao, he met with reporters at the station and made a statement, saying, "My resignation from Qingdao this time had unavoidable difficulties. After arriving in Weihai, all parties sent telegrams to retain me, and representatives from this city tracked me down and forced me to return to Qingdao. I am also very grateful for Chairman Han's joint telegram urging me to return, so I had no choice but to return to Qingdao. I am deeply ashamed and uneasy for the trouble everyone has taken to welcome me today. Qingdao still has many difficulties. On the one hand, I will temporarily take responsibility and continue to handle municipal affairs, and on the other hand, I will still resign to the central government and recommend a capable person to take over." (July 23)

The Ministry of Internal Affairs Urges All Provinces to

Establish County Government Experimental Zones 94

The Measures Will Be Implemented After Approval by the Central Government

Jiangsu, Shandong, Hunan, Hubei, Chahar, Shanxi, Yunnan, and Other Provinces Have Already Implemented This

Beijing Dispatch: In order to reform county administration and develop the rural economy, the Ministry of Internal Affairs previously planned to establish county administration construction experimental zones in appropriate locations in various provinces, with the aim of concentrating human and financial resources and, based on the needs of various undertakings, determining priorities and urgency, formulating detailed plans, conducting practical experiments, and gradually promoting them. Therefore, the Ministry drafted measures for the establishment of county administration construction experimental zones in various provinces and submitted them to the Second National Internal Affairs Conference. After repeated discussions by the heads of civil affairs departments and experts from various provinces, they all agreed that this was indeed an effective way to improve county administration. The General Assembly decided to pass it, and the Ministry of Internal Affairs forwarded it to the Executive Yuan for approval. Since the close of the Internal Affairs Conference, those provinces that have established such experimental zones or experimental counties include Jiangning Autonomous Experimental County in Jiangsu Province, Heze Experimental Zone in Shandong Province, Dingxian Experimental Zone in Hebei Province, Xiaogan Experimental County in Hubei Province, Xiangtan Experimental County in Hunan Province, Binyang County Experimental Zone in Guangxi Province, Yangqu and other Experimental Zones in Shanxi Province, and Bimin and other Experimental Counties in Yunnan Province. In addition, Zhejiang and Chahar provinces are also in preparation. Now, the Executive Yuan has forwarded the original measures for the establishment of county administration construction experimental zones in various provinces drafted by the Ministry of Internal Affairs to the Ministry of Internal Affairs, the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Finance, the Office of Political Affairs, the Health Department, and other agencies for joint review, and has revised the original measures appropriately and submitted them to the Central Political Conference for approval and implementation. The original text of the measures is transcribed as follows:

Measures for the Establishment of County Administration Construction Experimental Zones in Various Provinces

(I) General Principles 1. In order to improve the lives of local people and realize local construction, each province may establish county administration construction experimental zones (hereinafter referred to as "experimental zones") in accordance with the provisions of these measures. 2. The scope of the experimental zone shall, in principle, be based on a county unit, but it may be expanded to several counties if necessary. 3. After the experimental zone achieves significant results, it should be promoted to other counties at any time. If necessary, it may be approved to establish training institutions within the experimental zone to be responsible for training various construction personnel for use in handling county administration construction in other counties. The measures shall be determined by each province based on local conditions and reported to the Ministry of Internal Affairs for verification and record. 4. In order to compare the effects of the experiments and to facilitate observation, each province may establish two or more experimental zones in areas with different customs and practices. 5. The selection of the experimental zone shall be qualified if it has one of the following conditions: (1) The situation in the area can represent the general situation of the province; (2) The transportation is convenient and the location is appropriate; (3) The previous management of autonomy has been more successful; (4) There are local leaders who are capable and willing to contribute and support; (5) The experimental site has considerable equipment. 6. The selection of the experimental zone and the general outline of the plan in each province shall be decided by the provincial government meeting. 7. When each province selects the experimental zone and decides to establish it, the provincial government shall announce the location, scope of jurisdiction, and progress steps of the experimental zone and report it to the Ministry of Internal Affairs for submission to the Executive Yuan for record. 8. The Provincial Autonomy Preparatory Committee shall be responsible for assisting in the investigation of matters related to the progress of the experimental zone.

(II) Organization and Authority 9. The authority of the county government in the experimental zone should be expanded compared to the authority of the general county government. If necessary, a County Administration Construction Committee may be established to gather experts to be responsible for investigating the facts, formulating plans, training talents, and conducting on-site experiments. The organizational measures of the committee and the county government shall be formulated by the provincial government and submitted to the Ministry of Internal Affairs for approval and record. 10. The administrative scope of the experimental zone shall be the responsibility of the county magistrate in a county, and the responsibility of the county magistrates in each county shall be responsible in more than two counties. If necessary, a district office may be established, with one district chief in charge, to take overall responsibility for all administrative matters in the experimental zone. 11. The county magistrate or district chief in the experimental zone shall be selected by the provincial government from qualified personnel with excellent knowledge and rich experience. The district chief shall be a simplified position, and the appointment procedures shall be carried out in accordance with the provisions of the County Magistrate Appointment Law. 12. The reorganization or expansion of the county government organs in the experimental zone and the organization of the district office shall be formulated by the provincial government in detail and submitted to the Ministry of Internal Affairs for submission to the Executive Yuan for record. 13. If the implementation of central and provincial laws and regulations in the experimental zone is found to be difficult, it may be changed at its discretion, but it must be submitted to the central government for approval and record. 14. The experimental zone may formulate various individual rules as needed. 15. The scope of authority of the experimental zone is as follows: (1) Those that belong to the county according to laws and regulations; (2) Those that do not belong to the county's authority but have experimental nature; (3) Those specially assigned by the higher-level government. 16. The authority of the experimental zone and the province, the administrative power of the state, and the local autonomy power shall be clearly divided. The measures shall be formulated separately. 17. The county in the experimental zone shall establish a people's representative organ in accordance with the law before other counties to implement supervision of finance and review regulations to establish the foundation of democracy. 18. The county in the experimental zone whose autonomous undertakings have reached the degree prescribed in Article 8 of the National Founding Program shall be a county that has completed autonomy, and its people shall have the right to directly elect and dismiss officials and the right to initiate and veto laws.

(III) Funding 19. The funding of the experimental zone shall be allocated from more than 50% of the local income. The local income mentioned in the preceding paragraph shall be limited to the various items of local income listed in the standards for handling budget revenue and expenditure promulgated by the National Government on November 2, 1931. 20. If the funds of the experimental zone are insufficient in addition to the income stipulated in the preceding article, the provincial government should be requested to provide a subsidy from the provincial treasury as appropriate. All original surcharges and exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes should be exempted or reorganized. 21. All undertakings that belong to the province's operation or experimental undertakings with the same nature throughout the province shall be funded by the provincial treasury. 22. The experimental zone should pay attention to public utilities and use its income to manage local public undertakings. 23. All public property in the experimental zone shall be managed by a separate local property committee. 24. The experimental zone should implement a budget system and prepare a budget and final account statement on a regular basis and submit it to the provincial government for approval. 25. The finances of the experimental zone should be made public and the method of unified collection and expenditure should be strictly implemented. Absolutely no agencies are allowed to arbitrarily divide or misappropriate funds.

(IV) Implementation Methods and Procedures 26. The implementation procedures of county administration in the experimental zone shall be divided into the following two periods: (1) Administrative consolidation period, such as consolidation of financial administration, public security administration, and education administration; (2) Local construction period, such as surveying land, building roads, improving agriculture, promoting cooperation, adding schools, popularizing education, and providing medical relief facilities. The work in the above two periods must be carried out in an orderly manner. In the first period, the focus of the work should be on rectifying officialdom and eliminating accumulated abuses, and special attention must be paid to consolidating financial administration and public security administration. 27. The experimental zone may divide the whole area into several areas with different characteristics according to the conditions of transportation, culture, products, and social organization. In each area, select the central undertaking that is suitable for the needs of the local people and conduct experiments. 28. The county administration design and implementation matters of the experimental zone should pay attention to the following principles: (1) All facilities must be based on the needs of the real environment and the level of the local people, without emphasizing form or seeking quick results; (2) The implementation plan should first consolidate the matters that have been promoted, eliminate passive obstacles, and avoid unnecessary changes; (3) Cooperate with other specialized groups and institutions at any time and any place to carry out joint activities (4) Train people and cultivate talents from various experimental undertakings; (5) Local administration and autonomous personnel should strive to reduce written reports, form filling, and impractical slogans, and must go deep into the countryside to find ways to relieve the suffering of farmers; (6) Pay attention to the organization of people's groups, guide the people to implement autonomy; (7) Adopt the integrated method of (politics), (education), (wealth), and (health) to realize the entire plan and seek the restoration of the countryside in appropriate steps (8) The method should be simple and popular to reduce the burden on the people and to seek the benefit of the majority of the people; (9) The implementation of all undertakings must have the spirit of experimentation so that it can be promoted to other counties in the future.

(V) Supplementary Items 29. If there are any matters not covered in these measures, the Ministry of Internal Affairs may propose revisions at any time. 30. These measures shall be implemented after approval by the Executive Yuan. 31. Before the implementation of these measures, if each province has similar organizations of county administration construction experimental zones, their original names, measures, and related rules may be temporarily approved for application if it is inconvenient to change them. However, the provincial government shall announce the handling process and organizational situation and submit the measures and rules to the Ministry of Internal Affairs for submission to the Executive Yuan for record.

Hunan Province Holds Short-Term

Loan of 500,000 Yuan 95

Used for Road Construction and Radio Station Construction

Borrowed Proportionally from Seven Banks in Hunan Province

Changsha Dispatch: Hunan Province recently held a national salvation public bond of 5 million yuan for the purpose of resisting Japan and suppressing bandits, which has been approved by the central government and is now urgently being allocated to various counties and cities. In addition, a construction public bond of 10 million yuan was held for the purpose of clearing the old debts of China and Communications Banks and building the Baohong light railway. Zhang Gongquan and others from the Shanghai banking community came to Hunan last time, and all the procedures have been negotiated, waiting for the central government to approve and implement it. The central government is currently reviewing this. In addition, Finance Director Zhang Kailian and Construction Director Yu Jichuan were ordered by Chairman Chiang to complete the Xiangdong Highway within a time limit to facilitate suppression. At the same time, He Jian, in order to obtain timely military information, ordered the installation of long-distance telephones and the construction of a radio broadcasting station, which required more than 500,000 yuan in total. The two directors, Zhang and Yu, were unable to apply funds due to the provincial treasury's shortage and overdue party and government expenses for more than five months, and the matter was related to bandit suppression, so it had to be done. Therefore, they had to borrow 500,000 yuan from all seven banks in Hunan Province to deal with the situation. The draft loan agreement has been drafted by both parties and submitted to the provincial government for approval and record, and the funds will be delivered at the end of this month, starting from August 1, with a limit of ten months to clear the principal and interest. The loan agreement is as follows:

Regular Loan Agreement: Hunan Provincial Department of Finance and Department of Construction are now borrowing funds from the following banks for the purpose of building the Xiangdong Highway, installing long-distance telephones, and radio broadcasting stations, and the agreed conditions are as follows for compliance: (1) The total amount of the loan is 500,000 silver dollars; (2) The repayment period is from the date of signing the loan agreement, and every full month, 50,000 yuan and its interest shall be repaid, with a limit of ten months; (3) The monthly interest rate is 1.2%, and the interest decreases with the principal; (4) Repayment guarantee: The Hunan Coastal Salt Affairs Inspection Office is responsible for allocating 50,000 yuan and its interest every month and handing it over to the Bank of China for proportional repayment to each bank. The Inspection Office shall send a letter to each bank stating the allocation and apply to the general office of the Inspection Office for record and notify each bank for safekeeping; (5) Number allocation: Bank of China undertakes to borrow 150,000 yuan, Shanghai Bank undertakes to borrow 150,000 yuan, Bank of Communications undertakes to borrow 50,000 yuan, China Agricultural and Industrial Bank undertakes to borrow 50,000 yuan, Hunan Provincial Bank undertakes to borrow 50,000 yuan, Juxingcheng Bank undertakes to borrow 25,000 yuan, China

Industrial Bank undertakes to borrow 25,000 yuan; (6) Representative bank: The borrowed funds shall be publicly recommended by the borrowing banks to the Changsha Bank of China as the representative bank, and shall be distributed to the borrowing banks on the same day after each repayment is received; (7) This agreement shall be made in ten copies, and each relevant party shall hold one copy for safekeeping. The above conditions have been agreed by all parties and strictly complied with, and have been filed with the Hunan Provincial Government. Borrower: Hunan Provincial Department of Finance, Hunan Provincial Department of Construction, Borrower: Bank of China, Shanghai Bank, Bank of Communications, China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, Hunan Provincial Bank, Juxingcheng Bank, China Industrial Bank, Allocator: Hunan Coastal Salt Affairs Inspection Office (July 23)

Anhui Province

This Year's Budget is Prepared 96

Total Revenue and Expenditure Can Barely Match

Anqing Dispatch: The Anhui Provincial 22nd Annual Budget was passed by the Provincial Government Standing Committee last week. The total amount of revenue and expenditure was 11,173,934 yuan, and the revenue and expenditure could barely match. The budget for the previous year was 9,210,000 yuan for both revenue and expenditure. Later, the National Government Accounting Office ordered that the central government's assistance of 1,200,000 yuan be added to the approved revenue and expenditure, which were listed as 10,412,739 yuan. The first draft of this year's budget showed a very large increase in expenditure compared to the previous year, and the budget review committee discussed and stipulated three standards for reduction: (1) The organs that were originally established and had a budget in the previous year shall not exceed the budget amount of the previous year; (2) The organs that were established in the previous year but did not have an additional budget shall be prepared according to the minimum amount; (3) The newly added expenditures in this year shall comply with the instructions of the Headquarters and must first raise funds before increasing. Finally, after repeated reductions and revisions by various agencies, the draft was submitted to the meeting for review, and the total expenditure was still more than 11,100,000 yuan, which was still more than 1,300,000 yuan less than the total revenue of more than 9,800,000 yuan. The capital of the Four Provinces Farmers Bank of 500,000 yuan, the rural cooperative business fee of 120,000 yuan, and the public science museum of more than 70,000 yuan were increased by order of the Headquarters, and the debt fee of more than 560,000 yuan that had been paid in the previous year had to be increased in fact, and the remaining original funds could not be reduced. The only way to consolidate the original income of the Department of Finance is to increase the annual land tax by 250,000 yuan, the business tax by 100,000 yuan, the brokerage tax by 40,000 yuan, the slaughter tax by 70,000 yuan, the livestock fee by 30,000 yuan, the sanitary land price payment by 100,000 yuan, the official property reclamation by 160,000 yuan, and the road construction surcharge by 12,500 yuan, totaling 762,500 yuan, which can be used to offset the previous shortage, but there is still a difference of about 600,000 yuan, so it is planned to issue 600,000 yuan of treasury bills, which are specifically designated for the capital of the Four Provinces Farmers Bank and the rural cooperative business fee. The preparation of the business budget is set at 455,017 yuan, which has been prepared by the Department of Finance in two categories, ordinary business, and submitted to the Provincial Government Standing Committee for approval, and the Department of Finance will rush to prepare a formal budget and submit it to the Headquarters for approval and implementation. As for this year's special construction fee, it is heard that the fee for rice and photos has been cut off, and there is no designated fund to point to, and it is heard that the two departments of finance and construction will negotiate separately on handling it. (July 25)

Songjiang

Hurricane Passes Through, Seawall Rescue 97

Li Yihua, a seawall patrolman of the seawall works department in this county's Pudong area, was instructed by the Department of Construction and the county government that there would be a hurricane passing through on the 22nd and 23rd, and that the seawall works should be carefully protected, and the county government sent technician Zhao Shuda to the worksite to make arrangements. Unexpectedly, the seawall in that area was hit by a hurricane on the morning of the 22nd, originating from the southeast, and became more rampant in the evening. The patrolman immediately led more than 30 workers to rescue the seawall. The flood was almost level with the seawall surface, and the danger was very serious. The first to fifth sections were the most important. They used pre-set sacks filled with mud to selectively fill the gaps and depressions to make up for them. They worked all night, and the seawall danger subsided when the tide receded and the wind slowed down on the 23rd.

Wuxi

Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Opposes Increased License Tax 98

Zhu Qi, the newly appointed director of the tobacco and alcohol license tax collection office in this county, plans to double the collection of tobacco license tax starting in the autumn. After hearing the news, the industry stated that the Ministry of Finance's Taxation Department had issued a notice that the license tax should still be handled according to the old regulations, and the Jiangsu Stamp Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau had reduced the Wuxi tax amount to 80% this year, and the Shangbao tobacco and alcohol license tax was only collected at 2 yuan per quarter, so they unanimously expressed their opposition. Yesterday afternoon, they convened a temporary member meeting and resolved: (1) Send a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce to forward a letter to the collection office to strive to maintain the original amount; (2) Before obtaining a satisfactory reply from the collection office, in accordance with the methods of the same industry in various counties, each firm shall send the original paid license tax amount to the guild for transfer to the County Chamber of Commerce for preservation to maintain the national tax, and at the same time request the County Chamber of Commerce to forward a letter to the collection office to exempt the overdue reminder fee, and request the Public Security Bureau to forward a letter to all branches to suspend sending police to assist in the collection before the tax amount is resolved. After the discussion, they immediately sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce to forward a letter to the collection office to strive for it.

Agricultural Inspection Group Visits Wuxi for Observation 99

The Guangdong Zhongkai School of Agriculture and Engineering was founded by Madam He Xiangning, the wife of the martyr Liao Zhongkai. Min Weizhi, the captain of the first squad of the Shazhou Lao Haiba County Police Team, together with Chen Yanyi, a water police inspector, etc., seized over five hundred taels of opium carried by boatmen Song Lao Si and Wang Xiao Lao Guan in Xinqiao Baoquanxu on the 22nd at 10 PM. Patrol Chief Accidentally Shoots and Injures Civilian 101

Liu Lao Bazi, an inspector from the Xianzheng Narcotics Investigation Office, accompanied by Patrol Chief Du of the Water Police and a dozen armed soldiers, went to Dai Zhenru's house in Tangtou to search for drugs. Finding no evidence, they arrested Dai's wife. Just as they reached the west side of the street, they encountered Ni Guorui, a brick carrier, who had one hundred and four taels of opium. Qingjiang

Residents of the Second District Come to the City to Petition 102

Qiu Zixiao, Chen Chunhua, Wang Zhide, Gao Meicheng, and other male and female representatives, four to five hundred people in total, from Fuhe Township in the second district of Huaiyin, came to the county government yesterday (the 22nd). They claimed that their township chief, Sun Yaochuan, was oppressing the people and extorting contributions under the guise of grain storage. The donation amount was divided into four grades, with the highest being ten yuan and the lowest being one yuan. If there was no cash, it would be replaced by grain, and those who violated would be detained and fined. Having already petitioned the city once before, they went to the county government again yesterday with a petition requesting County Magistrate Pan to dismiss and severely punish Sun. County Magistrate Pan agreed to investigate and deal with the matter strictly. The petitioners then dispersed.

Pinghu

Forcing Daughter-in-Law to Death, Neighbors Request Justice 103

Ke Xu, from Sandengqiao in this city, works as a procuress in the women's prison and is known for her fierceness. Her daughter, Xingzhen, also has her mother's temperament. A woman named Huang rented a room in their house, and Huang had a beautiful daughter named Qibao. Xingzhen was envious and jealous of Qibao's poverty and often mocked her. The other day, Xingzhen's wickedness resurfaced, and she started a fight. Ke Xu helped her daughter and tore off Qibao's trousers. Onlookers applauded and laughed. Qibao, feeling ashamed and indignant, committed suicide by swallowing raw opium that day. The next day, the authorities were notified for an autopsy. The officials believed that Ke and Xingzhen were suspected of forcing her to death and immediately arrested them. Ke Xu was released on bail. The shops and neighborhoods believe that Ke Xu is violent and is still free from justice, so the community is upset and drafted an official complaint today and are requesting strict legal action from the county government.

Hangzhou

Prosecution Initiated in the Case of Brutal Murder of a Farmhand 104

Qi Zhongbao, a farmer from No. 6 Caoshe, Kuoshi Banqiao, West Lake, discovered that his daughter, Xu Qi, was having an affair with a monk named Xinkong. The farmhand Shen Afa caught them. Qi preemptively attacked, brutally killing Shen with thirteen cuts from a kitchen knife and burying the body in the vegetable garden to cover up the crime. The crime was leaked by a temporary worker, Qi Demao, and the police unearthed the body. The perpetrators were arrested and sent to court for trial. After investigation, it was determined that Qi Zhongbao was already seventy years old and could not have killed the strong and robust Shen Afa. His son, Amao, had a knife wound on his finger, making him undoubtedly the actual perpetrator of the murder. Qi Xu was also a co-conspirator in the murder. Both were charged with the crime of joint homicide under Articles 42 and 282 of the Criminal Law and were prosecuted according to law. Xu Zhan's adultery with monk Xinkong could not be substantiated, and she was declared innocent and granted immunity from prosecution.

Page 11

Local News: Navy's Domestically Made Jiangque Aircraft

Flew from Nanjing to Shanghai Yesterday 105

Landed at Hongqiao Airport, Welcomed by All Sectors

Will Continue Northward Flight After Replacing New Engine

Will Fly Back to Shanghai from Beiping, Then Fly South to Hong Kong and Guangdong

Chen Wenlin, Director of the Xiamen Naval Aviation Department of the Ministry of the Navy, accompanied by Pan Dingxin, Head of the Mechanical Section, flew the domestically-made military land-based training and reconnaissance aircraft Jiangque, departing from Xiamen on the 20th and flying across the country via Fuzhou, Wenzhou, and Liyang. They arrived in Nanjing on the 21st. Due to slight engine damage, repairs were completed yesterday morning. They took off from Nanjing at 2:45 PM yesterday and arrived at Hongqiao Airport at 4:50 PM. They are scheduled to stay in Shanghai for three weeks, replace the 120-horsepower engine, and then fly north. Details are as follows:

Arrived at Hongqiao

Director Chen and Section Chief Pan departed from Xiamen on the 20th, passed through Fuzhou, Wenzhou, etc., and arrived in Nanjing on the 21st. They originally planned to fly to Shanghai the next day, but after inspecting the aircraft, they found that the engine was slightly damaged. They worked to repair it, and it was completed yesterday morning. They left Nanjing for Shanghai at 2:45 PM in the afternoon. Between Changzhou and Suzhou, they encountered sudden rain twice, so they ascended to an altitude of 6,000 feet to avoid the rain. They arrived in Shanghai at 4:50 PM and landed at Hongqiao Airport. Few people knew about Chen's flight to Shanghai in advance. Only Zeng Yijing, Director of the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant, Lin Wojiang, Secretary-General of the Aviation Association, and more than a dozen reporters from various newspapers went to welcome them.

Engine Replacement 106

After Director Chen deplaned, Director Zeng invited him to a small room next to the airport for a light refreshment. Then they went back to the airport to watch the performance of the Italian Fiat Company's fighter plane to take pointers from the performance. The Jiangque aircraft's current engine is 85 horsepower, which is not suitable for long-distance flights. Therefore, it has been decided to replace it with a 120-horsepower engine in Shanghai. The engine has been selected by the British Far East Aircraft Company and will be replaced by personnel from the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant here. It will take about three weeks to complete the installation. Director Chen and Section Chief Pan are currently at the Naval Entertainment Club and will wait for the engine replacement to be completed before continuing to fly to North and South China to complete the feat of circumnavigating the country.

A Glimpse of the Fuselage 107

The Jiangque aircraft fuselage is painted silver. The upper wing has the Blue Sky with a White Sun emblem. At the rear, the rudder has vertical stripes of blue and white. On both sides of the front of the fuselage are the emblems of the Naval Aviation Department. On both sides of the rear of the fuselage are the words "Jiangque." The upper and lower wings are staggered, unlike the parallel upper and lower wings of foreign aircraft. The fuselage is extremely light. One person holding the tail can push it quickly. The entire aircraft is constructed with extraordinary precision.

Cost 10,000 Yuan 108

The total cost of manufacturing this aircraft is about 10,000 yuan, which is one-third cheaper than foreign aircraft. If more are built, it can be even cheaper. After it was completed this month, the team decided to make a long-distance flight across the country to attract people's attention so that the Chinese people could witness the state of domestically made aircraft. After the first test flight, the results were excellent. The people of Hong Kong also came to Xiamen to visit. On the morning of the 20th, Director Chen and Section Chief Pan departed from Xiamen on the aircraft, passed through Fuzhou and Wenzhou, and reached Liyang, Jiangsu, staying overnight. They flew to Nanjing on the 21st.

Aircraft Manufacturing Process 109

Yesterday, our reporter at the airport interviewed Chen Wenlin. Chen, wearing a naval uniform, was humble, energetic, and about thirty years old. He was indeed a promising young man. He introduced Pan Dingxin and spoke eloquently about the process of manufacturing the aircraft. Chen said, "Section Chief Pan and I were classmates in Germany. Seeing that most of our country's aircraft were purchased from Europe and the United States, we worked hard to study and design in detail. Section Chief Pan has special expertise in mechanical engineering, and we finally succeeded. Therefore, the style is different from imported products in several places, but it is more convenient and sophisticated." All materials, except those that our country lacks, are made domestically. The engine was dismantled from the Xiamen aircraft, which I flew back to China from Germany four years ago. The others are newly built. It took about three months, and only five or six people were manufacturing during breaks. If we raise special funds and hire workers to build, the time can be shortened."

Staying in Shanghai for Three Weeks 110

After arriving in Nanjing, we originally planned to fly to Shanghai immediately, but the engine was slightly damaged, so we stayed in Nanjing for repairs. It was repaired this morning (yesterday morning) and arrived here at 4:45 PM in the afternoon, taking only two hours. The aircraft is 85 horsepower. If it is replaced with a more than 100 horsepower engine, the flight will be faster. The fuselage is more than twice as light as foreign goods, so turning up and down during flight is particularly fast, which is very satisfying. It is planned to stay in Shanghai for three weeks to replace the 120-horsepower engine.

The Jiangque Aircraft Flying from Nanjing to Shanghai (Photo by Gong Shuma) 111

Nationwide Flight 112

After the installation is complete, the team will fly north, scheduled to go through Bengbu, Xuzhou, Jinan, and reach Peiping. From Peiping, the team will fly to Tianjin, Qingdao, and return to Shanghai, then fly south, passing through Xiamen, Hong Kong, Guangzhou, and other places to complete the nationwide flight. I hope that the people of the whole country will jointly advocate the self-production of aircraft, then we can plug loopholes, and the country's strength is hopeful."

Sun Not Coming to Shanghai 113

Finally, the reporter asked about the news of Sun Tonggang, the aviator who recently flew from Germany to Beijing. According to Chen, "I met Sun twice in Beijing. Sun's long-distance flight from Germany back to the motherland was indeed arduous. I also flew the Xiamen aircraft from Germany along this route four years ago. Sun and I studied aviation in Germany and were classmates. When I left Germany, Sun had just arrived in Germany to study German. Now Sun plans to fly to Jinan within a few days to visit relatives. His flight route is not planned to go through Shanghai."

Kan En, Foreign Exchange Broker

Views on the Silver Agreement 114

Limited Benefits for Relevant Parties

Little Impact on the Shanghai Market

The Ta Mei Wan Bao reported that Kan En, a foreign exchange broker in this city, is known among foreigners as an authority on silver. Recently, he expressed his opinion on the silver agreement of the World Economic Conference, believing that the signing of the agreement still has limited benefits for those related to silver. A world conference should not only focus on such one agreement, which must be regarded as a great achievement, but its actual benefits are also limited. It cannot achieve unexpected results for silver. The so-called sacrifices made by Spain, India, and China are not real sacrifices. India has always sold no more than 35 million ounces of silver a year. Now it is allowed to sell this quota every year. Spain has never exported silver, but now it can sell 5 million ounces every year. China has not actually exported silver in terms of import and export differences, except for the past six months. Moreover, one point that has not been paid attention to in the agreement is that speculators in New York currently hold 122.5 million ounces of silver. Once they dump it on the market, it will be like dropping a bomb. As for the agreement's impact on the Shanghai market, it will have little impact, partly because its impact has been preemptively offset and partly because its effect is not sufficient to guarantee the future of silver and its permanent strength. If China believes that this agreement will stabilize the silver market, it is not something that ordinary psychology can understand. Because the silver price is still fluctuating as before, and how can the silver price be stabilized when the gold price is not stable?

Java Taipan Comes to China

Investigating Commerce in Central Java 115

Supplementing Java Sugar Production for Transport to China. Rescuing Shipping in the South Seas

Competing to Transport Northeast Miscellaneous Grains for Export

Java sugar is transported to our country, with annual shipments of hundreds of thousands of tons, selling well in various places north and south of the Yangtze River. However, after the January 28th Incident, imports decreased significantly. After the import tax was increased, Java sugar coming to China declined even more drastically. Shipping was also greatly affected. Mr. J. Nieuwenhuys, General Manager of the Java Shipping Company, came to Shanghai to investigate the commerce of various places in our country in order to prepare to supplement shipping to China. The reasons for the decline of Java sugar are recorded as follows:

Decreasing Shipping Volume 116

Our country has purchased Java sugar due to years of resisting inferior sugar. The amount transported to Shanghai alone is always between 300,000 and 400,000 tons. The Java Shipping Company specially opened eight South Seas liner ships to transport Java sugar to Shanghai. Before the outbreak of the January 28th Incident, Java Shipping alone transported more than 250,000 tons of Java sugar to Shanghai in the previous year. Last year, various places in our country were affected by the aggression of a strong neighbor, and all industries were depressed. Java sugar also reduced its shipping to China. This year, since the customs increased the import tax on sugar, the tax is more than the sugar price. Those who are managing Java sugar stopped buying. Although the sugar price has repeatedly fallen, because the tax rate is too large, transporting sales to China is encountering greater setbacks. According to Java Shipping Company statistics, the sugar loaded in the first six months of this year is less than 50,000 tons, which is only 30% of the year before. Recently, inferior sugar has been transported along the Yangtze River. Java sugar may become even more depressed in the future.

Limiting Production 117

Java regards sugar as the bulk of its production and China as its only market for sales. Now that Java sugar cannot be smoothly transported to China, the sugar factories are piling up with inventory. Although the price has been reduced to 4 guilders per picul, there are few orders due to the heavy tariffs, resulting in a situation of surplus sugar. The Dutch government, in order to help Java sugar merchants, has limited the production volume. It is also planning to sell Java sugar, designating it to be sold exclusively by one company, which is equivalent to a monopoly method, to avoid repeated competition and indiscriminate price drops. After this news spread, most of the Chinese merchants operating sugar in Java rose up in opposition. If this matter is realized, the South Seas sugar merchants will inevitably go bankrupt completely, so this matter has not yet been realized.

Inspecting the Northeast 118

The products of our country that are sold to the South Seas Islands are mostly Northeast soybeans, soybean cakes, and miscellaneous grains, all of which are transshipped in Shanghai for export. Since the Northeast was forcibly occupied by Japan, the Northeast soybeans and other goods transported to the South Seas have disappeared from Shanghai due to the tax levied by the puppet state and are now directly transported to Java from Dalian. Japanese ships have taken over 70-80% of the shipping rights. The Java Shipping Company only sends one ship to Dalian per month, and its business has also suffered significant losses. This time, Java Taipan Nieuwenhuys personally went to the Northeast to investigate the export situation of soybeans and miscellaneous grains, preparing to increase the number of ships to compete with Japanese ships and make up for the losses.

Improving Passenger Seats 119

Most of the overseas Chinese doing business in the South Seas are from Fujian and Guangdong, so the Java Shipping Company's Xiamen passenger tickets are a huge business. Every time a ship travels to and from Xiamen, there are often three to four hundred overseas Chinese on board. Recently, the Dutch government has increased the head tax for Chinese entering the country to 150 guilders per person. If there is no proper guarantee when entering the country, they are not allowed to land. They must also pay a population donation every year. After the company's ships twice had incidents of crew insulting Chinese passengers, each ship has now authorized each Chinese compradore to improve treatment in order to maintain the business in that port. Today, the Taipan Nieuwenhuys has decided to take the Jinan ship to Xiamen to discuss with the local branch manager the improvement of treatment for Chinese passengers and the convenience of taking ships in order to eliminate the accumulation of bad habits.

Confirmed in this city

Germany Building Bombers for Us 120

Inopportune To Release Details

Guo Wen She reported that the foreign cables are saying that a German factory is building bomber and fighter planes for China, the first batch is thirty aircraft. Reporters sought information regarding this and it is indeed a fact but before the time is right, they can't release more details.

Duan Qirui's Illness Has Gradually Recovered 123

Duan Qirui's illness is currently being treated by Dr. Finner, the German director of internal medicine at Baolong Hospital, and Dr. Wang Jianggao, a former doctor at Baolong Hospital. Ministry of Finance

Appropriating Funds to Expand the Aircraft Manufacturing Plant 124

Director Zeng Requested the Ministry to Quickly Allocate Funds to Add Factory Buildings and Machinery

Maximizing Expansion Can Produce 100 Aircraft Per Year

The Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant has been striving to expand and actively develop since it moved from Mawei to Shanghai in the spring of 1931. Director Zeng Yijing had drafted a plan and submitted it to the Ministry for adoption. It has been approved by the Central Political Council and funds have been allocated for expansion. Details are recorded as follows:

Drafting a Plan 125

The Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant in Gaochangmiao occupies about 100 acres, bordering the Huangpu River to the east and the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway to the west, with convenient water and land transportation. Director Zeng Yijing had drafted an expansion plan, initially for 300,000 yuan, with 80,000 yuan for building factory buildings and 220,000 yuan for adding machinery. As for the detailed methods and factory building drawings, they have all been decided. After the expansion, six aircraft can be manufactured each year, and it has been submitted to the Ministry of the Navy for approval.

Approved Appropriation 126

After the expansion plan was submitted to the Ministry, Yang Shuzhuang also submitted it to the Central Political Council, which approved the appropriation of more than 100,000 yuan for expansion. It was submitted to the Military Affairs Committee for review and transferred to the Ministry of Military Affairs for handling. The Ministry of Military Affairs decided to submit it to the Aviation Administration for consideration. After the Aviation Administration reviewed it and attached its opinions, it was submitted to the Executive Yuan, which ordered the Ministry of Finance to allocate funds appropriately. The Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant recently submitted a request to the Ministry to request the Ministry of Finance to quickly allocate funds in order to proceed.

Current Situation 127

A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency recently met with Director Zeng, who said that after the Ministry of Finance allocates funds to Shanghai, he will immediately find ways to expand, first building factory buildings on the open space in front of the gate and adding power machinery. Because most of the original machinery is manual, there are currently 100 workers, all of whom are skilled workers. The engineers are all students who graduated from the United States and naval training. Only one aircraft used on the Ninghai warship is currently being manufactured. As for the current situation, due to financial difficulties, expenses are kept to a minimum. For example, the salary of engineers is no more than 200 yuan per month.

After Expansion 128

Since the establishment of the business department in this plant this year, it has been dedicated to designing drawings and manufacturing various types of commercial and military aircraft for all sectors. It will also use domestic materials as much as possible to ensure that customers are satisfied. However, since its establishment, no one from all sectors who are enthusiastic about promoting aviation has ordered from the plant. After the initial expansion, the annual output can be increased to six aircraft, and the manufacturing will be faster. It is hoped that all sectors will come to order, the price is low, and the quality is excellent. We welcome the outside world to come to the factory to monitor the work. If the funding is sufficient, given the size of the land, building a factory for manufacturing can produce up to 100 aircraft per year.

The Municipal Council Cracks Down on Rubber Factories

The Machinery Industry Association Submits a Protest 130

The Industry Association Pushes Representatives to Urge Inquiries with the Municipal Government

The Machinery Industry Association submitted a document to the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating, "This submission is for the matter of petitioning. Since the implementation of our country's Factory Law, the Shanghai Public Concession Taxpayers' Association unilaterally amended Article 34 of the appendix to the Yangjingbang Land Regulations. The Association knew that the Municipal Council was deliberately destroying our country's entire labor administration and resisting the right of factory inspection so that it could not be implemented within the concession area. Later, due to repeated opposition from various groups in Shanghai, knowing the excitement of our people, they changed their strategy and sought shortcuts, citing Article 30 of the Yangjingbang Regulations to prevent public danger as an excuse, ordering Yiyuan and other factories to stop work and relocate. Article 30 has been established for a long time, why not implement it in the past but apply it today? Its sinister intentions are known to everyone. If it once indulges its power and plunders our right to inspect factories in the concession, there will be many disadvantages, which are listed as follows: (1) The concession authorities protect foreign merchants' factories from inspection by Chinese officials. (2) Increase the Municipal Council's large amount of licensing revenue. (3) Understand Chinese industrial secrets. (4) Suppress Chinese industry, making it impossible to develop. (5) Destroy China's entire labor administration, making it ununified, and it is also convenient to make excuses for other negotiations. According to the above situation, it concerns national sovereignty. It is appropriate to protest reasonably to protect sovereignty and ensure industry, which is in the public interest. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Industry of the National Government."

The Rubber Products Industry Association of this city held a standing committee meeting at 2 PM yesterday, chaired by Shi Zhishan. The resolutions were: (1) Chairman Shi submitted that the application of the new member, the Da Zhongyang Rubber Factory, to join the association has been pending for a long time and has not yet been investigated. Now, at the 23rd standing committee meeting, the case was submitted for reconsideration, and the standing committee members Shi Zhishan, Shen Mengshi, and Mao Yuting were appointed to investigate the factory in detail. The report showed that there was nothing inappropriate and asked whether it could be approved to join the association. The resolution was that since it has been verified that there is no suspicion, it should be approved to join the association. (2) The National Goods Factory Federation and the Rubber Industry Union of the Third District inquired about the handling of the case of the Municipal Council ordering the relocation of factories. The resolution was to reply separately that the case has not been resolved yet, and the three members Feng Yunchu, Yang Weiyin, and Shen Mengshi will be pushed to the Municipal Government to urge inquiries. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM.

The City's Busy Season Silver Tax to Begin August 1st 131

The Municipal Land Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating: "Notice regarding the city's busy season silver tax for the 22nd year, scheduled to begin on August 1st. Concerning the tax quota for the Zhenru District, previously, due to reports of a poor autumn harvest in the 21st year, a request was made to reduce the land tax to provide relief. The Finance Bureau, together with this bureau, investigated the disaster situation and agreed to a general reduction of 0.05 of the busy season grain tax. This reduction was not implemented in the same year, and it was proposed to offset it against the 22nd year's busy season grain tax. This proposal was submitted to the municipal government and approved. This bureau has complied with the instructions on record. The busy season silver tax for this district in the current year should be reduced by 0.05 according to the approved plan. The remaining districts will continue to collect taxes based on the old amount and price, with detailed information recorded on the tax bills. It is stipulated that all taxes must be paid within two months from the start of the tax collection period, with a deadline of September 30th. Those who fail to pay by the deadline will be subject to an additional 0.2 tax. An additional two months will be allowed, with a deadline of November 30th. Those who still fail to pay by the deadline will be subject to an additional 0.1 tax as a penalty for late payment. This matter has been reported to the municipal government for record-keeping and has been communicated to the relevant departments. A notice is hereby issued to inform the people of this city to pay their taxes at the counters within the specified time limit, obtain receipts, and secure their property. Do not delay. This notice is urgent."

Negotiations Underway Regarding the Tounan Case

Order from the Ministry of Transportation 136

The case of the China Merchants Bureau's Tounan vessel being sunk by the Japanese vessel Changchun Maru, resulting in the drowning of over a hundred people, has been submitted to the Ministry of Transportation by the bureau based on the report of shipowner Jiang Changqing for review and instructions. At the same time, a letter was sent to Gao Tingzi, Director of the Navigation Administration Department, stating that all important documents and orders would not be published until formal negotiations have been initiated. Yesterday, the Ministry of Transportation issued an order to Shanghai, stating that the exact number of passengers who died in the sinking of the Tounan and the full extent of the vessel's public and private losses have not been reported in detail. Furthermore, the bureau has not reported on the steps taken in negotiations with the Japanese merchants or the progress of the situation. As this matter involves international negotiations, the bureau is ordered to submit a detailed report immediately to allow for review and handling and to prepare for serious negotiations with the Japanese side. The bureau has completed the preparation of Jiang Changqing's detailed report in Western languages and will submit it to the Ministry of Transportation for review.

Shipowner's Statement 137

Shipowner Jiang Changqing recently issued a statement in response to a letter sent by passengers rescued from the Tounan to the shipping ticket office, claiming that the shipowner and crew did not carry out rescue operations after the accident. The statement reads: "The Tounan vessel was split into two sections immediately after being struck by the Changchun Maru. I was trapped under the bridge and, after being pulled out, saw that the front section of the vessel had already sunk. Eight passengers and twenty-nine crew members on board jumped into the Japanese vessel. I was the last person to leave the Tounan. If I had jumped immediately upon impact, I could have jumped to the deck of the Changchun Maru with thirty others. Why would I have been holding onto the hatch? Furthermore, the Tounan sank in only four minutes. If rescue operations could have been carried out, why would Erche Zheng Jingsheng have returned to the cabin and drowned? The radio operator rushed into the cabin to retrieve a life jacket and was trapped inside. If the waves had not destroyed the cabin, he would have also died. At that critical moment, with the ship sinking in an instant, how could rescue operations have been possible? If the ship had not sunk completely in four minutes, wouldn't the fifty-three crew members, all experienced sailors, have preferred to escape rather than be buried in the bellies of fish? Shipowner Jiang also stated that the rumor that the Tounan sank after twelve minutes was completely false."

Tragic State of Banditry in Sichuan 138

The Chinese Red Cross Society recently received a joint report from refugee groups in Bazhong, Tongjiang, and Nanjiang counties in Sichuan Province, stating: "The scourge of the Xu Kuang Red Bandits has spread to Sichuan, and our three counties of Bazhong, Tongjiang, and Nanjiang have suffered greatly. Since last year, we have been invaded repeatedly. The brutality of the massacres, the scale of the destruction, and the completeness of the looting are well-known to officials. Prosperous areas have been transformed into desolate wastelands in an instant. Now, we have fallen into misery again. The people of our three counties are constantly falling under the iron hooves of the Red Bandits, or wandering homeless in the ditches of foreign lands. Neighboring counties have tens of thousands of refugees gathered. The cries of the refugees are endless, and there is no way to survive. We earnestly plead with kind-hearted people to embrace a spirit of compassion and show mercy. We ask you to donate grain, provide porridge, draw water from the West River, or gather quilts to distribute to the refugees in various areas to provide relief and revive the survivors so that the refugees of our three counties can return to their homeland and see the light of day again. We would be eternally grateful. We submit this urgent plea in the hope that you will understand." The society has been involved in Sichuan relief for many years, and the people are grateful. Now, the banditry in Sichuan has begun, and the suffering is extreme. According to reports, the situation is appalling. The refugees are desperately crying for help. Unfortunately, the society has received little funding and is unable to cope. How can we acquire thousands of rooms and millions of bushels of porridge to save these surviving refugees who are awaiting death? Compatriots with compassion, will you rush to their aid?

After Water Level of Yangtze River Declined

Yellow River Swells Again, Danger Reported 145

The water levels in various sections of the Yangtze River have been declining daily, and it is hoped that the flood season can be passed safely. However, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, which is responsible for the dike work in Hubei Province, is still actively carrying out flood control work. The Engineering Department of the National Economic Council in this city received a report from the Jianghan Bureau yesterday stating that a light railway was used to transport soil to repair the dangerous section of the Qikou Dike in Huangmei County. A sub-dike has been built and internal supports have been added to the seepage area of the Shangchewan Dike in Jianli. Wave protection work has been carried out on the Dayue Dike, and board piles have been driven and internal supports have been added to the leaking sections. Stone has been thrown on the outer slope of the Zhoujiahe River Dike, and earth supports have been built on the inner slope. Sub-dikes have been built at Zhusangong and Jiangjianaodeng to prevent seepage. The Xiang River area has also been secured after emergency protection measures were taken. The Engineering Department also received a telegram from the Henan Provincial Works Bureau stating that the Yellow River has swelled rapidly, the third dam of the Luo River has been washed away, and the water level has suddenly risen by four to six feet, posing a serious danger.
