Police Interference with Clothing Store Hawking 147

Taxpayers Association Seeks Justice for the Industry

The Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Public Concession sent a letter to the Public Works Department yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of clothing store hawking, we have received your replies of July 8th and 15th, which have been forwarded to the Shanghai Clothing Industry Association. We have received a letter from the association, acknowledging receipt of your letter of July 5th and awaiting the Public Works Department to correct the actions of the police hired with taxpayers' money. However, we have also received a joint letter from Hongyu, Tiansheng, Qiantai, Hongtaixiang, Guchang, Shuntai, Fuyuan, Fulai, Xiekang, Hengxing, Yuanshun, and other clothing stores, stating: 'We have received and reviewed your previous letter to the association and understand that it has been forwarded to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Chinese Taxpayers Association for forwarding to the Public Works Department. Our fellow merchants on this road have been repeatedly harassed by the Huishan Police Station. Since our previous letter to the association, we have been prevented from hawking three times and have been forced to pay fines in court twice. If this continues, our shops will be unable to withstand the disturbance. Not only is our business disrupted, but we fear that our industry's future livelihood will be interrupted. At 4:00 PM on the 8th, Police Officer No. 29 from the police station came to each house to prevent us from hawking, recording our door numbers. This happened during a time when customers were plentiful. The police suddenly dispersed the customers and ordered us to turn over our clothes. Our fellow merchants did not dare to resist and had to let them do as they pleased. Clothing stores operating in the concession are taxpayers. Why are we not protected but instead harassed? We have no choice but to request that your association uphold justice, quickly provide assistance, and engage in serious negotiations with the police station. We also earnestly request that you forward our letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Chinese Taxpayers Association to provide assistance in maintaining our business and alleviating our business difficulties. We have communicated this matter accordingly and request that you investigate and assist. Thank you.' We understand that your association sent a letter to the Public Works Department before July 5th. The department should uphold its repeated declarations to respect the wishes of the citizens and, based on the value of taxpayers' money being used to purchase peace, immediately correct the actions of the hired police. However, at 4:00 PM on July 8th, Police Officer No. 29 still went to each house to prevent hawking and ordered them to turn over their clothes, continuing to engage in destructive business practices. This not only failed to implement the declaration to respect the wishes of the citizens but also violated the principle of taxpayers' money being used to purchase peace and disregarded your association's letter. Therefore, we are writing again to request that you quickly negotiate with the Public Works Department. Otherwise, our association will send another letter to your association, convening a representative assembly of Chinese taxpayers to discuss the issue of taxation in the future. We have informed you of the reasons for this. Please reply as soon as possible. We understand that maintaining traffic is important. However, since the Hongkou area was allowed to be used as a military base by the Japanese army last year, commerce has declined. The clothing stores in the area are attempting to improve their business by adopting advertising methods, which is commendable. If it is believed that hawking truly obstructs traffic, it may be better to first consult with the industry association through this association to find a mutually agreeable solution. Imposing penalties hastily is more likely to create misunderstandings. The association's plan to request this association to convene a representative assembly to discuss future taxation issues has its reasons. We have informed you of the reasons for this. Accordingly, we request that your association absolutely refrain from interfering with clothing store hawking as much as possible, provided that it does not impede traffic."

Opposition to Rent Increase on North Fujian Road 148

Lao Gongmao Bank Announces 10% Rent Increase

City Federation and Others Petition Party and Government to Stop It

Most of the shops and residences on North Fujian Road are properties managed by the rental department of the Lao Gongmao Bank. Recently, the bank suddenly announced a uniform rent increase of 10%. The tenants opposed this increase, citing the poor market conditions and their inability to afford it. They requested assistance from the 37th Branch of the First Special District City Federation and the Road Merchants Association. Lao Gongmao then sent a letter to the two associations, proposing to send representatives to discuss the rent increase. The two associations sent five people, including Sun Wenyi, to negotiate. The two sides initially agreed to temporarily increase the rent by 5%. However, Lao Gongmao suddenly sent a letter denying the previous agreement. Therefore, the two associations held a joint meeting and decided to firmly oppose the rent increase and insist on their opposition. It is said that they will petition the party and government organs to issue a strict order to stop it.

Jisheng Society Donates Medicine to Aid Disaster Victims 149

200 Bottles of Newly Invented Emergency Shasha Dan

The Chinese Jisheng Society has recently invented and prepared an eye corner Emergency Shasha Dan to treat Susha disease, which is very effective. When encountering an emergency Susha, apply this medicine to the four corners of the eyes. After application, tears will flow, and the eyes will feel very painful. The limbs will become numb and cold. The medicine will then directly reach the dantian, and the symptoms will be relieved. If there is no pain in the eyes after application, then it is not Susha disease. However, it must not be ingested. One bottle of this Dan can treat three or four people. Apply it two or three times every two minutes until the patient's limbs are no longer numb or cold and the body feels comfortable. Therefore, the society donated 200 bottles of this medicine to the Shanghai Charity Organizations Relief Northeast Refugee United Association yesterday, requesting them to be forwarded to the two resident directors of various charity organizations, Dong Qu Yingguang and Feng Yangshan, for use in relieving the sick and poor in the disaster area. It is said that the association will send the medicine to the post office for distribution.

Lawyer Xu Shihao Covered in Feces 150

丨A Hooligan Prank丨

Lawyer Xu Shihao went to the Second Special District Court at 9:00 AM yesterday to represent Shi De in the case against Wang Zhenchuan and others for trademark infringement. After the court session, Xu left the court at 10:30 AM, carrying a briefcase. As he stepped out of the gate and was about to open the car door, a tall man with a Northern accent, wearing a xiangyunsha shirt and trousers, was standing outside the court. When he saw Xu leaving the court and opening the car door, the man went up to greet him. Xu nodded in response. Unexpectedly, the man took advantage of Xu's leaning over to get into the car and dumped half a watermelon rind full of feces on Xu's head, completely covering Xu's straw hat, white silk long gown, and the car door and interior with feces. The stench was unbearable. The man stood still and did not leave. Two Westerners went up to him, grabbed him, and sent him to the police station. Upon arriving at the police station, the police chief questioned the man, who only gave his name as Zhang Debiao, 30 years old, from Tianjin. When asked why he threw filth at people and who instructed him to do so, Zhang remained silent. The police chief ordered him to be detained pending investigation and sent to court for trial. In the afternoon, Xu reported the incident to the police station and requested a thorough investigation into the instigator and the arrest and interrogation of the culprit.

Retrial of Case of Killing Stepmother

Zhang Wenqing Sentenced to Life Imprisonment 151

Zhang Wenqing, a woman from Huzhou, instigated Chen Wencai and others to kill her stepmother, Zhang Su, at her residence on Route Carde in western Shanghai two years ago. The police station filed charges. As a result of the initial trial, Zhang Wenqing, Chen Hengcai, Gao Jintang, and Yao Yonggui were all sentenced to death. Zhang and others were dissatisfied and filed an appeal. At the conclusion of the second trial, Chen Hengcai was still sentenced to death, but the sentences of the other three defendants were reduced by one degree and each was sentenced to life imprisonment. However, the prosecutor and the police station who filed the charges in the second trial felt that the sentences were too lenient and appealed to the Supreme Court in the third trial. After reviewing the case files, the court overturned the second trial's judgment and sent it back to the Higher Second Branch Court for retrial. The court has been convened multiple times recently. Zhang and the other two male and female defendants were all brought before the court, and witnesses were summoned for questioning. Yesterday morning, Judge Yu, along with judges Zhao and Jiang, took the stand to announce the verdict. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu and the defendant's defense lawyer both appeared in court. Judge Yu then announced the judgment, stating that Zhang Wenqing was guilty of instigating and plotting murder and was sentenced to life imprisonment. Chen Hengcai and Gao Jintang's appeals were rejected. Yao Yonggui's portion was not accepted. After the judgment, the police sent the three defendants back to the men's and women's prisons for imprisonment.

Woman Poisons Herself with Three Yuan 152

Ying Ye, a woman from Ningbo, 49 years old, whose husband passed away several years ago, has a son named Gen Cai, nearly twenty years old, a carpenter. The mother and son lived at No. 119 Yongji Lane, Dongxi Huade Road. The day before yesterday afternoon, Gen Cai asked his mother for one yuan in pocket money. His mother told him to take it himself from the box where she kept the money. Later, Ying discovered that three yuan was missing from the box and suspected that her son had taken it. She questioned Gen Cai, who firmly denied it, leading to an argument. Afterwards, Ying became resentful and despondent, and secretly swallowed opium in a suicide attempt. Her son discovered her and found that she was barely breathing. He immediately sent her to Guangren Hospital for treatment, but to no avail. She soon died. The hospital reported the incident to the Huishan Police Station, who sent detectives to investigate. They then transported the body to the Feilun Road autopsy center. Yesterday morning, they reported the matter to the First Special District District Court, which dispatched a prosecutor to the center to examine the body. The prosecutor interrogated Ying Gen Cai, who recounted the events. The prosecutor then declared that the deceased, Ying Ye, a female, had died from opium poisoning. Her son, Ying Gen Cai, signed a statement to take the body back for burial.

Momentary Lapse Leads to Descent into a Fiery Pit 154

Gu Gendi's Letter Reporting Her Experience of Being Driven to Learn Opera

Liao Zhuanji Seeks Assistance from the China Relief Association

Gu Gendi, the twenty-year-old wife of Liao Zhuanji, a tin worker residing at No. 2, Huikang Lane, Caiyang Lane, outside Xiaonanmen in the Nanshi district, was quite beautiful. Three years ago, an old woman from a barber shop in the same neighborhood falsely claimed that she could learn opera and lured her to sell her services as a prostitute at the Xinchun Courtyard of Lao Si in Xiacun Street, Zhangzhou, Fujian Province, for a price of four hundred yuan. Since losing his wife, Liao has searched for her everywhere, but there has been no news. On June 9th of this year, he suddenly received a letter from Gu, which stated, "To my husband, Zhuanji, with deepest regards: Due to a moment of foolishness, I was deceived by an old woman who brought me to Zhangzhou, initially saying that I would learn to sing opera. Little did I know that I would be sold into the brothel world. At that time, I was helpless and had no relatives. I had no choice but to make the best of a bad situation. As of today, I am in debt for about four hundred yuan. A momentary lapse has now left me ill, and the suffering in my illness is beyond words. I only hope that my husband will remember our love as husband and wife and find a way to get me out of this fiery pit. I would be forever grateful. I am writing to apologize and beg that you reply as soon as you receive this letter. Wishing you peace. Your wife, Gu Gendi." Upon receiving the letter, Liao was both surprised and overjoyed. However, the travel expenses were too high, so he hesitated. In the past few days, he has received several urgent letters describing her pitiful situation, which chills him to the bone. Liao has been trying to raise travel funds for days, planning to go there, but few have responded, and he seems dazed. Some have suggested that Liao write a letter to the China Relief Association on Longmen Road to request assistance. After receiving the letter, Chen Angui, the director of the relief section of the association, questioned Liao in detail about everything. Because the matter was in Zhangzhou, it was inconvenient to take sole responsibility. He submitted it to a regular meeting of the association, which immediately decided to send someone to Zhangzhou to investigate in order to negotiate and reunite Liao with his wife.

Apprentice Crushed to Death by Giant Log 155

Zhang Jinlin, a thirteen-year-old apprentice at the Daxingxiang Tobacco and Paper Store at No. 72 Dongbaoxing Road, Shenjiawan, Zhabei, a local, went to urinate in the Zixiang Lane across the street after getting up yesterday morning. A giant log placed by a carpenter's shop next door, leaning against the wall, was suddenly blown down by the wind. The log fell and crushed Zhang Jinlin's head, causing his brains to splatter, and he died instantly. Someone witnessed the incident and called the police, who sent him to Tongren Hospital by car before transferring him to the morgue for examination.

Special Mention

Municipal Facilities After the War in This City (Continued) 167

B. Educational Administration (A) Regarding School Education (1) Repairing the school buildings of municipal schools. The school buildings of municipal schools in the Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong war zones were mostly burned down. Except for the school buildings of Jiancheng and other schools, which were completely burned down and could not be built due to the city's financial difficulties after the war, the remaining schools have been repaired one after another. (2) Adding school supplies and teaching aids. The necessary items for each school have been roughly equipped, but books and instruments still need to be supplemented. (3) Restoring municipal schools in the war zone. In addition to the five schools, Jiancheng, etc., a total of 29 primary and secondary schools have been restored. (4) Taking over private primary schools. Schools in the war zone suffered damage. Private schools, in particular, found it difficult to sustain themselves. Therefore, the two private schools, Huaide Primary School and Xitang Primary School, applied to be taken over by the city. After investigation, it was confirmed that the two schools were indeed necessary to maintain, so they were approved to be changed to municipal schools. (5) Adding municipal primary school grades. Dexin and other 14 schools added grades, and Maicun and other 5 schools added teaching assistants. (6) Providing relief to primary and secondary schools in the war zone. The first phase approved 40,000 yuan for private registered secondary schools in the disaster area and 10,000 yuan for municipal primary and secondary school subsidies. The second phase is in progress. (7) Implementing the war zone revival education plan. (B) Regarding social education, (1) restoring people's supplementary schools and simple sports fields. People's schools, supplementary schools, and simple sports fields in the districts of Jiangwan, Wusong, Jianbei, Yinhang, Pengpu, Zhenru, and Yinxiang have been repaired. (2) Restoring the Wusong Reading Room. The Wusong Reading Room temporarily rents民房 to restore the library building before designing and constructing it. (3) Repairing and adding public reading boards. 11 public reading boards in various districts have been repaired and 39 new ones have been made. (4) Preparing for the city center library. The regulations for the preparatory committee for the municipal library in the city center are being drafted.

C. Financial Administration (A) Regarding the restoration of tax collection agencies, the tax collection agencies that were suspended due to the war include (1) the Municipal North Inspection Office, (2) the Yinxiang Inspection Office, (3) the Wusong Ship Donation Office, (4) the Zhabei Ship Donation Office, (5) the Xiaoshadu Inspection Office. The above five agencies have been reorganized and restored successively after the withdrawal of the Japanese army. (B) Regarding the organization, reduction, and exemption of taxes and public properties. (1) Houses in the Zhabei and other war zones were mostly burned down. The municipal government has separately stipulated reductions and exemptions to help the people in the war zone. (2) The residences of civilians in the first and third districts of Zhabei and the public houses in Wusong were mostly burned down or damaged. The Social Affairs Bureau and the Public Works Bureau have jointly planned to request funding for reconstruction or repair. (C) Regarding the planning of post-disaster and reconstruction funds.

(1) After the war, the city's income decreased sharply and its expenditures increased sharply. The municipal government planned 500,000 yuan for reorganization expenses. The Finance Bureau negotiated with the bank to overdraw 150,000 yuan, and the rest was raised by reorganizing tax revenue in non-war zones. (2) Issued 6 million yuan in public bonds for the revival of the disaster area to be used for the revival of the war zone. (D) Regarding the relief of the people in northern Shanghai after the war, the people in northern Shanghai after the war were in dire need of relief. The Finance Bureau consulted with the Shanghai Race Club, the China Jockey Club, and the International Sports Association to hold charity races and issue lottery tickets. 25% of the income was used for charity expenses.

D. Educational News Highlights Ministry of Education Will Form

Normal Curriculum Standard Committee 168

The Ministry of Education previously organized the Primary and Secondary School Curriculum Standard Committee to draft curriculum standards for various subjects in primary and secondary schools and kindergartens. However, the normal curriculum standards have not yet been discussed and determined. Now, normal education has become a system of its own. For example, Jiangsu and other provinces have separately established normal schools from those originally attached to middle schools as departments. Since normal education has a special place in the academic system, its curriculum training has its own special point of potential. It is necessary to gather ideas and benefit from each other to formulate appropriate curriculum standards. It is heard that the new curriculum standards announced by the Ministry of Education, in middle schools, still have subjects such as civics and geography under review. When the civics and geography subjects are announced, the middle school curriculum standards will be complete. Then the Ministry will begin to organize the Normal Curriculum Standard Committee to discuss and draft the Normal Curriculum Standards.

Jiang Shixun Talks

Examination Process of Middle Schools in the City 179

Planning to Award Scholarships to Students with Excellent Grades

The Exam Leakage Case Has Been Clarified, 31 Graduates from Jianguo

This year's joint graduation examination for primary and secondary schools in this city, the preliminary examination, follow-up examination, and supplementary examination have all ended successively. The results of the joint examination have also been announced. However, this joint examination is the first one held in this city, and the process of handling it is deeply concerned by educators. Yesterday, the reporter of the Shanghai News Agency visited Mr. Jiang Shixun, the executive member of the high school group of the examination committee, and learned about the process of this year's joint graduation examination for middle schools as follows.

Executive Committee Member Jiang Talks 180

This city's joint graduation examination for middle schools, after the dispute over the leakage of examination questions occurred, the follow-up examination and supplementary examination were held on the 13th, 14th, and 15th of this month and have been completed. The grading method follows the Ministry's order, with 40 points as the passing grade. This lenient approach is not due to the disturbances, but because it is the first time that a joint examination is held, it cannot be too harsh. The school should be responsible for the good or bad performance of the students, not just the students themselves. In total, this middle school,

Examination Results 181

Approximately 80% of the students in each subject passed and are allowed to graduate. Approximately 10% of the students failed in three or more subjects or were absent and are held back. The remaining 10% or so of the students failed in one or two subjects or were absent and should take supplementary lessons. Among the students who are held back or take supplementary lessons, the majority are absent. Only a small number of students actually failed. There are still some students who, either under the suggestion of the school or under the pressure of a few students, left the school and could not participate in this follow-up examination, totaling more than 180 people. These students may have already taken eight or six subjects, and there is still one or three subjects that have not been taken. They have been approved by the Ministry,

Temporary Enrollment 182

Starting from today, they can go to the Education Bureau to collect certificates of passing subjects taken in order to apply for schools. The certificate states that they still need to take supplementary examinations for the subjects not taken. The Education Bureau will stipulate the supplementary examination methods and dates, which will generally be before the start of school. If they still do not participate in this supplementary examination or fail the supplementary examination, their enrollment qualification will be revoked. The Education Bureau has already stipulated the calculation method for the overall results of this joint examination. Based on the school's grades, the ranking of the school and the ranking of the students will be revealed. For schools with poor performance, improvements will be made. Schools with excellent performance will be rewarded. The students with the best grades may

Award Scholarships 183

The specific methods still need to be submitted to the Bureau Affairs Meeting for approval before a decision can be made. The Education Bureau will compile a detailed report and explanation of all the detailed processes and grades of the joint examination, on the one hand to let the schools know the actual situation, and on the other hand to serve as a reference for the next joint examination. As for the

Pre-Examination Leakage 184

Case, the Bureau has sent 1,000 pieces of evidence to the Shanghai District Court. After the court's investigation, the prosecution has now been completed. The defendants are Zhang Jieliang, a proofreader from the Nanjing Printing Company, Xie Zhen from the Central Daily News, and Xie Ying, a student from Jianguo. As for the students from Jianguo Middle School who participated in the joint examination, except for Xie Ying, whose qualification was revoked, the rest have been announced, totaling 31 passing students, it is said.

University Education Association Submitted a Request

The Ministry of Education Approved Enrollment for the Law School 186

The Foundation of Private Schools Lies in Students

The Method of Reorganizing Education Lies in Daily Practice

Please Consider the Hardships of Starting a Business and Handle it Flexibly

The Shanghai University Faculty Association yesterday sent a telegram to the Nanjing Ministry of Education stating: Minister Wang, Nanjing Ministry of Education: We have recently received a statement from members of our association, stating that your Ministry issued an order on the 20th of this month to stop the Shanghai Law School and other schools from enrolling new students and transfer students, giving them a final opportunity to improve. This shows that your Ministry has the intention of actively encouraging improvement while passively cracking down. However, these schools have been established for many years, with painstaking efforts and arduous management, and have now gradually established a solid foundation and a basic scale. In the future, under the strict supervision and guidance of your Ministry, they can certainly be reorganized and innovated, in line with the expectations of your Ministry. We believe that the foundation of private schools lies in students, and the method of reorganization lies in daily practice. Now that enrollment is stopped, the classes will be interrupted, and the economic sources will be cut off. Maintaining the status quo is already difficult, and reorganizing the school affairs is even more difficult. There is fundamentally no opportunity for improvement, which is not the original intention of your Ministry to protect education. Therefore, we specially send a telegram to earnestly request your consideration of the schools' enthusiasm for running schools and the hardships of starting a business. We earnestly hope that you will handle it flexibly and allow them to continue enrollment, which would be fortunate for education. Respectfully submitted, Shanghai University Faculty Association.

Yesterday, I specially sent a letter to the directors of the various departments, asking them to reduce the minimum cost required again, and send it to the meeting together with the planning book of each department before the 25th of this month, so that it can be submitted for discussion at the second plenary session of the Preparatory Committee on the 29th of this month. According to the opinions of most of the preparatory committees, the cost of 50,000 yuan, no matter how frugal, will definitely be insufficient. Since the government is sincerely holding this meeting, it must also know the actual difficulties. Therefore, after the second meeting of the preparatory committee, it will immediately submit a request to the central government to increase the budget. At a minimum, it must be issued in full in accordance with the previous decision of the Executive Yuan of more than 90,000 yuan before it can be started. Otherwise, it will be difficult for a clever woman to cook without rice.

This conference is a great stimulus for the entire province. The Qilu athletes vowed to work hard to hone their skills and wait for the future. Recently, the sports field has been expanding the football and basketball fields, building a gymnasium, to prepare for the North China Football and Basketball Tournament during the winter vacation. The Education Department is also planning to build a swimming pool to train the navy. The recent preparations are described below.

Swimming Pool 203

This province has no such equipment for swimming, and there is no way to practice it. Therefore, in the past North China Games, only track and field and ball games were participated in, and swimming was just watching from the sidelines. The situation is similar to today's China, with an army but no navy. Last year, Jinan citizens requested the government to build a swimming pool, and the location was planned on the side of Yuequan Spring in Nanguan, but it was a flash in the pan and was shelved again. Recently, He Siyuan of the Education Department led the athletes to the Qingdao Games. Because there are swimming teams in many provinces and cities, the Shandong team, which lives by the sea, was absent, which is a great regret. After returning to Jinan, a swimming pool is now being planned. The location is planned to be at the Black Tiger Spring under the southeast corner of the Nanguan City. Because Jinan is known as the two famous springs, the water source is strong, and it can be set up everywhere. Once the plan is determined, construction can be started, and it is expected to be realized in August. Black Tiger Spring is a famous scenic spot in Jinan. The blue water is clear and transparent. There is a stone tiger head carved beside the spring. The spring water gurgles and spurts out of the tiger's mouth, splashing beads and jade, like the sound of waves on the beach. If a swimming pool is built there, it will complement the famous spring and be a natural scenic spot.

Soccer Basketball 204

The next North China Football and Basketball Tournament has now been confirmed to be held in Jinan during the winter vacation. Although the track and field field of the Provincial Sports Field has a rough scale, the ball field is still mostly simple. After the Qingdao North China Games, expansion is now being planned to prepare a place for the teams from the ten provinces and cities in North China to use their weapons. In addition to the original football field temporarily borrowing the track and field field, new foundations purchased in the east of the field are being sorted out. Five new basketball fields have been set up in the new field, and one football field is being built. It should be enough to use during the North China Football and Basketball Tournament. As for the old field, six tennis courts and four volleyball courts are also being renovated at this moment. Expanding the sports field, Zu Shangshu Mei told the reporter that the sports field plans to build a gymnasium (gym), the address is planned to be west of the current office, the old earth ditch is filled and built, and the scale is slightly imitated from the Tsinghua University gymnasium. There is a basketball court and office in the room, and it is still in the planning stage. Only after the decision is made can preparations begin. (20th)

Special publication

Recent Problems in the Lives of Japanese Elementary School Teachers (by Yuan Wenzhang) 205

1. The Arrears in Salary for Japanese Elementary School Teachers

Since the outbreak of the agricultural panic in Japan, the rural economy has practically entered a state of bankruptcy. The impoverishment of farmers has affected the living conditions of elementary school teachers. In some rural areas, teachers have even been asked to personally visit farmers to collect overdue taxes in order to pay the teachers' back wages. This situation shows that local governments in Japan are truly helpless in dealing with economic problems. According to a report by the Japan Imperial Teachers Association in April of last year, there were salary arrears in one prefecture and twenty-four counties (out of three prefectures and forty-three counties nationwide in Japan), totaling 381 schools. The situation was particularly severe in Kumamoto, Nagasaki, and Nagano prefectures. Today, although the problem of salary arrears has spread throughout the country, what was once considered "more severe" in places like Kumamoto is no longer uncommon. Here are a few examples:

A certain teachers' association in Niigata sent a report to all teachers in the county, stating: "When observing the real situation in rural areas and seeking to understand the dynamics of the educational community, everything feels stagnant and corrupt. The deepening of the agricultural panic has rapidly led to insecurity in the lives of six thousand rural teachers in our county. Due to the expansion of deferred tax payments, the salary arrears of teachers have reached more than thirty schools. Rural areas have also implemented forced donations and reduced bonuses, etc. Over one hundred and three schools in Akita Prefecture have salary arrears, amounting to over 100,000 yuan. Teachers have truly reached the lowest stratum of poverty..."

Comparable to the above report is a report from the county education affairs department on the situation at the end of last year. According to this report, twenty-four townships and towns had salary arrears, amounting to 27,000 yuan, with the village of Suizu in Sado being the most severe, having arrears dating back to April of the year before, continuing until the end of last year.

In Nagano Prefecture, the number of schools with salary arrears was twenty-eight in April of last year, seventy-two in May, and reached one hundred and eighty-six in June. Here is a statistical summary of the salary arrears situation in the county (June 1932):

Arrears

Number of schools: 425, 186

Number of teachers: 7,512, 2,716

Monthly salary amount: 418,000 yuan, 119,000 yuan

28.54%

In the northern part of Iwate Prefecture, there is not a single place that can pay full salaries. Most arrears are around three months. The Tokyo Asahi Shimbun's Iwate edition also reported that "When the county authorities sent personnel to various townships and towns to urge payment, the village chiefs, assistant officers, and accountants all avoided meeting them, so the authorities had no choice but to ignore the situation." In Miyagi Prefecture, salary arrears affected fifty-five townships and towns.

In other areas, although salaries are paid, various exploitative methods such as forced donations are used, which effectively amount to salary reductions. According to the recent "Survey of Rural Depression" by the Imperial Agricultural Association, many places still implement forced donations, ranging from one to six tenths of the salary.

2. The Compensation of Japanese Elementary School Teachers

The salaries of Japanese elementary school teachers were not originally high enough to warrant reductions. Consequently, everyone finds it impossible to make a living. The total number of elementary school teachers nationwide, including regular teachers in primary and higher grades, specialist teachers, associate teachers, and substitute teachers, is 234,700 (surveyed in March 1931). The average income of each teacher is 70 yuan, 2 jiao, 4 fen for male regular teachers in ordinary courses, and 49 yuan, 7 jiao, 4 fen for female teachers. When comparing the salary ratios of men and women in urban and rural areas, the ratio is 55% in urban areas and 45% in rural areas.

The above are average amounts. Now, let's talk about the highest and lowest. The highest-paid male regular teachers in core subjects earn 240 yuan, and female teachers earn 120 yuan. Male regular teachers in primary courses earn 130 yuan, and female teachers earn 100 yuan. The lowest-paid male teachers in core subjects earn 10 yuan, and female teachers earn 12 yuan. Male teachers in primary courses earn 15 yuan, and female teachers earn 8 yuan.

Spring and Autumn

Summer Vacation 206

— Yan

The scorching sun travels across the sky, green shade encircles the earth. During the hot summer, all major, middle, and elementary schools are on summer vacation.

The education authorities stipulate 42 days for elementary school summer vacation, 56 days for middle school, and more than two months for college. The heat is the same, but the length of vacation differs depending on whether the student is in elementary, middle, or college. Person A says: Because college students are most afraid of the heat, middle school students are next, and elementary school students are less so, therefore college vacation is the longest, middle and elementary schools are next. Person B says: Logically, college students are strong, and more heat resistant, vacation should be the shortest; elementary school students have not yet fully developed, they are very fragile, they can least endure the heat, and should get the most days off. Middle school students remain in between. Person C says: The older the student, the more they should read dead books, they should go to society to read live books, so the vacation should be the longest. Person D says: There should be no summer vacation at all, if you say you cannot read books because of the heat, then why do farmers not stop cultivating, workers not enter factories, merchants close their shops, soldiers not fight, or rickshaw pullers not pull cars because of the heat? Also, a vacation is not hot from the first day to the last, and a day is not hot from morning to night, on days that are not hot, cool mornings, you can read books, summer schools after summer vacation burst forth like bamboo shoots after rain, is that not clear proof that you can read books in hot weather? Person E says: There should be a summer vacation, but before the vacation begins, the school should assign them vacation homework, students in the countryside should be asked to do this, students in workers' districts should be asked to do that, students in the city should be asked to do this, one by one they take the homework outline and work according to the outline, and when school starts, each turns in the homework report, and the strengths and weaknesses are critiqued, this is an excellent grade, important learning. Today's schools, futilely give summer vacation, and never give them live books to read, wasting time, it is a pity! It would be better to not have vacation and give them more dead books to read.

The words of Person A, B, C, D, and E, who is right and who is wrong, please let the education world think.

Summer Scenery 207

— Huang Kewei

It's summer again. | These words slipped lightly from people's mouths.

On the skyscrapers, hangs a scorching sun, like a brazier.

The swimming pool is filled with a large amount of blue Shar, turning the water into a turquoise color. Water battles, hand-to-hand combat, laughter, scolding, chasing, are publicly exhibited, showing the beauty of lines, the beauty of health; a great new contribution of the summer of 1933 |

The beggars do not have the blessing of entering the swimming pool, and can only wash in the Suzhou River, but, the police came, and they ran away in a puff of smoke.

The banners of summer sales flutter scrapingly, the signs of cold drinks hang high, timely ornaments of the street ah!

Under the big yellow umbrella. Frozen sour plum soup has also come on the market, five coppers for a cup, an economical cold drink; Zheng Fuzhai's is good. | A friend said to another friend.

Under the pink cool umbrella, a soft waist trembles, like a flower snake.

In the big mansion, they are arguing about where to go for summer vacation: the third concubine wants to go to Lushan, the fifth concubine wants to go to Moganshan, the young master is clamoring to go to Sullivan, but the eldest young master wants to go to the Wusong seaside for a spin first.

In the evening, the benches in the park are full of people, buttocks touching buttocks; the cars on Jungong Road fly by in succession, the car's rear end stirs up dust, making people unable to breathe.

The sea is roaring, the street trees are swaying, the people enjoying the cool breeze are laughing!

It's summer again. | Life slipped lightly from people's mouths.

The scorching sun, drunk on whiskey, just returned from the city, face red, like a persimmon, stepping to the rhythm of a waltz, tilted and crooked, falling behind the dark mountain.

Under the bean trellis and melon racks, the farmers are shirtless, drinking white liquor, eating peanuts, content and at ease.

The fields send the singing of shepherds, the calls of cuckoos, the chirping of cicadas, the croaking of frogs. The children, naked, jump into the creek to take a clean bath and scoop up a bowl of snails and mussels, catch a few big fish, and go home to supplement dinner, truly fun.

The young village girl, steals a peek, blushes with shame, and quickly hides in the house.

The peaches are ripe, wonderfully red, climb up the tree to pick and eat, one, two, three

Smoke rises from the thatched roof, curling, like a black dragon, smearing the splendid rosy clouds black.

The summer in the city is noisy, filled with the stench of sweat and flesh!

The summer in the countryside is quiet, depicting a beautiful mood!

Fan 208

— Rong Yu

The fan fans a cool breeze, fans in summer, not winter. Someone asked to borrow it from me, wait until the middle of August.

These four lines of vulgar poetry, in elementary school students, shop clerks, and friends who know a few characters, are often seen on the fans they hold. Although the words are vulgar, the meaning is very practical. From the perspective of new literary scholars, it can be included in the book of folk literature. As for the refusal to lend the fan, the reason is very obvious. You are hot and I am hot; you want to fan yourself and I want to fan myself. Who would sacrifice their own happiness for the benefit of others? You invade other people's rights for your own happiness, which is not a good thing. So, not lending the fan, in terms of emotion and reason, makes sense. Moreover, "the fan follows the person." As you wave it and walk, you may forget to return it to the owner and fan it all the way to your home.

People with knowledge, after all, have more tricks. On the snow-white fan surface, they invite calligraphers and painters to brush a few strokes. In fact, it may not be cooler to fan with it. And because they cherish the calligraphy and painting on the fan surface, they are unwilling to fan it vigorously. This kind of fan, rather than saying it is a cooling item, it is more accurate to say it is an ornament.

Zhuge Liang on the stage always holds a feather fan, regardless of the cold winter or hot summer. This fan seems to be like the walking stick held by modern people, decorating the scene, and showing off the prestige. The oilcloth fan used by friends in the underworld is painted with Yama sitting high; a judge standing by; and little ghosts crowding on both sides. At first, I thought it was to encourage good and punish evil. Later, I realized that the painting contained a song, which is the rules for underworld heroes to join the gang. Although there is no restriction on the use of fans, there is a certain distinction in secret. Men mostly use bamboo-bone folding fans; women use goose feather fans and round fans; occasionally, they use small folding fans, which are only three or four inches long, so how can they fan out a breeze. Friends in the underworld and laborers like to use oilcloth fans; villagers like to use palm-leaf fans. I think palm-leaf fans have the largest breeze; the price is also the cheapest; and they are the most durable. Friends of practical philosophy can advocate the use of palm-leaf fans.

Elegy for Xilin 209

— Tao Zaidong

I received the obituary of Cen Xilin in June. Public opinion on the Duke has settled, and the national history will have biographies and eulogies. I am merely writing a private elegy. I accompanied the Duke when he served as the Minister of the Court of Judicature during the Guangxu Jiawu year of the Qing Dynasty. That year, war was declared with Japan. The Duke submitted a memorial requesting the gathering of the former troops of the late Duke Xiangqin to go out and kill the enemy. His loyalty, bravery, and indignation were expressed in the words "punishing the Japanese" and "conquering the dwarves," surpassing even today's anti-Japanese rhetoric. The imperial edict was issued to the Imperial Commissioner Liu Kunyi for dispatch. The Duke was displeased, and I also resigned. Six years later, during the Gengzi Boxer Rebellion, the Duke served the King in Xi'an, was appointed Governor of Shaanxi, and then transferred to Governor of Shanxi. I entered the Duke's staff for the second time. In Renyin, he was transferred to Governor of Guangdong, but he did not take office and was promoted to Governor-General of Sichuan. There were bandit disturbances in Sichuan, and he was ordered to proceed with all speed. He left Taiyuan on the 15th of July and arrived in Chengdu on the 24th of August. The imperial court praised his speed, and the French minister especially admired him. I was one of those who followed the Duke with all speed. I was thirty years old at the time, and the Duke was about forty years old. The accompanying civil and military officials were all young people, with no one over fifty years old. At that time, people said that the staff of the commander-in-chief were all children. The journey followed the Hedong Road, crossed the Yellow River at Lingfeng Ferry, entered Tongguan, passed Xi'an, crossed the Wei River, took the road through Fengxiang, and entered Sichuan along the Jialing River from Guangyuan and Zhaohua. I gained the richest poetry from this expedition. Just as the Duke was taking office, a telegram arrived informing him that his wife had passed away in Hubei, and his son, De Gu, had also died. To this day, I still don't know why this event has remained so deeply etched in my mind. The following year, I was recommended by Teacher Dai Wencheng for a special examination and entered the capital. I resigned for the second time. After that, I met him once in the old capital, and again in Shanghai. During the eighth or ninth year of the Republic of China, I encountered him in Shanghai. The conversation was filled with even more feelings of vicissitudes than before. The decline of the country and the demise of people, alas! The students and former officials will surely hold a memorial meeting. Among those whom the Duke recruited, I should be the first, and also the least successful. Sighing for the departed, I also reflect on myself. A hundred thoughts converge, and I am lost in confusion. Afflicted by illness, I am unable to go and mourn. I hastily write this elegy, the words of which are:

The nation's troubles are repeated, finally breaking away from the world like an old woman, closing her eyes and no longer seeing. Old journeys are vivid, remembering the scattered guests of those times, my tears are hard to hold back.

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 210

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twelve: The Poor and Humble Join the Army, the Sick Fall Behind

Sacrifice is Sweet to Resign, Soldiers are Sentimental

But my nerves were excited, but they didn't listen to people's commands. Outside the window, the sound of wind passing through the sky, and the sound of dead branches being broken by the cold wind and hitting the roof tiles. The snoring in the soldiers' rooms came in waves, reaching my ears. Since my ears were not deaf, and I was awake, there was no way I couldn't hear the sound. Since I heard every sound, I naturally couldn't sleep. I don't know when, I used some magic tricks to make myself meet Guizhi. Guizhi was dressed even more beautifully today, wearing a pink long dress, and under her black hair, she had a red flower stuck in it, which set off her appearance with a kind of joyful aura. Could it be that she was getting married? If she was getting married, then of course she would marry me. As he thought this, it seemed that Guizhi had guessed his thoughts, and read his mind like a torch. She glared at him and said: "Don't have those dreams, do you think I can marry you?" Zhao Ziqiang exploded. Whether she married me or not was not important, but why did she put on such a proud appearance? So he said: "It's not like I'm making this up, there are people who can act as matchmakers to prove it. You've suddenly changed your mind, could it be that you're going to marry Master Gan? You should know that he's so poor right now that he can't even find a bowl of rice, and I'm the one who came up with a way for him." Guizhi said: "Don't slander people behind their backs, I'm determined to marry him. Listen, he's here with the flower car to pick me up. Isn't that the music team playing?" When Zhao Ziqiang heard this, he listened carefully, and sure enough, it was the bugle playing. However, the bugle call was not a love song, but the reveille. Zhao Ziqiang suddenly sat up with a start. Oh my! Where was anyone getting married? It turned out he was just dreaming. There was no need to think about it, he quickly got out of bed. A company commander is always much freer and more comfortable than a soldier. Just after Zhao Ziqiang got out of bed, his orderly had already entered the room to make his bed and bring him water to wash his face. (139)

Small Gardening

Lotus Talk 211

— Zhu Kui

Under this sun, which is as scorching as a flaming umbrella, the lotus leaves are standing tall and turning over the whole pond of green clouds. The white and red lotus flowers are even more like fairies floating on the water, shaded by the green leaves. Their graceful figures and subtle fragrance permeate the breeze, as if sitting opposite a noble person, and all mundane influences disappear. Mr. Zhou Dunyi said well: "Emerging from the mud unsullied, washing in clear water and self-cleansing." In fact, the virtue of the lotus is not limited to self-preservation! The hotter the sun, the more spirited the flowers bloom, standing upright under the scorching sun. This indomitable spirit of resistance is not only the hero among flowers, but also our model. Perspiring while talking about lotuses, to fulfill the small gardening of Spring and Autumn. The types of lotuses The most common lotus flowers are the red lotus and the white lotus. Red skirts and plain clothes, reflecting the lush green canopy, like the goddess of the Luo River, gliding gently on the waves, elegant and serene, truly indistinguishable from poetry and painting! The petals are numerous, growing in clusters like a plate, which is a double-petaled lotus flower. Most of these flowers are red lotuses. They are magnificent, but unfortunately, they do not bear lotus pods. One stem with two flowers is called "twin lotus"; the multi-talented and ill-fated Feng Xiaoqing once wrote in her ashes: "...I wish to use a drop of willow branch water to transform into twin lotus flowers in the world." One stem with three flowers is called a trinity lotus. In addition, there is a double-layered lotus flower, in which another lotus flower blooms from the lotus pod inside after the outer lotus flower has fully bloomed, just like a multi-storied building. There are also blue lotuses and water lilies. I have never seen a blue lotus, but water lilies are foreign varieties. The flowers are white, light red, or light yellow, floating on the water surface, about half the size of Chinese lotus flowers.

Cultivation of lotuses Lotuses are root-born plants; their roots are lotus roots. The cultivation method is mostly to leave the lotus seedlings in the mud, letting them grow on their own. For those planted in jars, during the plum rain season, first spread river mud as fertilizer on top of the lotus seedlings, and dry them in the sun. When the river mud cracks, then pour water and continue to expose them to the sun. The green leaves and red flowers will grow rapidly and bloom. However, for lotus flowers in jars, first, there must be no shortage of water after watering. The amount of water should be gradually increased to maintain a balanced amount. Second, no more fertilizer should be added. My friend, the painter Mr. Liu Junran, has three jars of double-layered lotus flowers in his studio. This year, after adding water, because he felt that the leaves were not large enough, he added some river mud. Unfortunately, the lotus flowers that were already budding in two jars withered and died. The foods of lotuses The lotus flower petals can be used to make flower dew. Lotus seeds and lotus roots, in addition to being eaten raw; cooked lotus seeds can be made into candied lotus seeds and lotus seed paste. Lotus roots can be cooked into dishes, or stewed into cooked lotus roots and lotus root flour. (Mash old lotus roots and filter the juice. After the starch settles, mix it with boiling water to eat. It is fragrant and delicious, far superior in taste to the lotus root flour sold in the market.) Lotus nodes and lotus roots can also be used in medicine. The steamed chicken and meat with fresh lotus leaves are even more delicious dishes in the summer.

Suzhou's lotuses Outside Suzhou's Fengmen gate, the Huangtian lotus roots, and the ten miles of lotus ponds, with red lotuses reflecting the sun and green leaves suspending clouds, have long become the only scenic spot in Suzhou in the summer. The fat, crisp, and tender lotus roots, famous throughout Jiangnan, are produced there. In the gardens, the Su Yuan of Jinde Road used to have trinity lotuses and twin lotuses discovered, but unfortunately, they have not bloomed for a long time. In addition, because the lotus pond in the Humble Administrator's Garden is still large, lotus flowers can still be viewed. The Lingering Garden and Canglang Pavilion, etc., mostly have only ordinary red lotuses, and they are not very lush. In recent years, the lotus flowers in the park have indeed become more prosperous and numerous because a pond has been added. In the early morning or at night, go to the Dongqi Teahouse to drink a pot of clear tea, and the elegant fragrance will be gently carried over, making you feel like you are floating into the sky. Unfortunately, there are too many vulgar guests in the park, who are competing for pursuits of both sexes. How many among the thousands can appreciate the refined interest of lotus flowers? Alas!

Free Talk

"Edited" and "Authored" 212

— Another Realm

Frankly speaking, the value of editing a book is not lower than authoring one. Especially in China today, where the cultural level is extremely low. For more than a decade since the New Culture Movement, the general youth are still infatuated with the circles of classical Chinese poetry and martial arts and love novels. Not only have various scientific theories not produced much achievement, but even the new literature has not been deeply understood. The popularity of Spring Love Novels is a clear proof. (It is a big mistake to think that vulgar triangular and quadrilateral love novels are only read by shop clerks.) So, the people who are now carrying the task of the cultural movement, instead of specializing in trafficking foreign masterpieces, why not spend part of their energy to do some rehashed editing work for a wider range of people to read? Its significance is more far-reaching than the former. This is the first. Secondly, there are very few who can truly engage in research using scientific methods. Moreover, due to the shortness of time, it is impossible to produce mature works. Even the few academic monographs that are currently attracting attention are nothing more than borrowing from the achievements of foreign research, and the so-called application of materialistic dialectics is especially full of errors. Therefore, if we simply "abandon the fundamental and pursue the superficial" and thoroughly edit and write foreign masterpieces, the editors will be able to obtain beneficial lessons, and the readers will benefit more than reading raw and unrefined local products. This is another reason why I say editing is not lower than authoring.

However, the edited and written products in the publishing industry today cannot satisfy people. The reason is probably that the general editors are forced by life and do not have enough time to search and collect in detail, but only hope to gather a few more pages of manuscript paper and calculate how to exchange a little more living expenses. The result is a patchwork, and its worthlessness is obvious. This is the reason why the current edited and written products cannot be valued.

When I was teaching in the North, I felt a steady difficulty. The general youth have a new desire for knowledge and hope to read some theoretical books, but they cannot understand the many hard translations that are currently available. Recently, I heard that these books have no sales at all, which proves that there is room for discussion in this road. I think it would be best if there could be a book of famous masterpieces that summarizes and simplifies the many profound theories. This is the task of the editor.

"Multiple Dam Collapses in the Upper Reaches" 213

— Li Youran

Switzerland has many mountains. The mountains are so close together that a person cannot step across. The Swiss build suspension bridges (Pont Suspendu).

| | The bridge is suspended in the air between the mountains. When the gentle feet of a woman walk across, the bridge will shake as if it is about to break; when a heavy car passes, the bridge will only shake, but it will not break. Therefore, with such bridges, Switzerland, which is as beautiful as a large "rockery," is even more beautiful, and the Swiss are famous for building suspension bridges.

The Netherlands has a lot of sea. The sea is higher than the land, and when the tide comes, | | people will be swept away. The tide comes often; but have all the Dutch been swept away? No. They often admire the wonder of the sea being higher than the land because they are most famous for building dikes.

In short, Europeans also encounter many natural disasters and many obstacles, just like the Chinese; but they overcome them and transform them into magnificent sights.

The flooding of the Yellow River in China is a famous natural disaster since ancient times.

Yes, this is a famous natural disaster since ancient times, everyone knows it. But to this day, whenever the Yellow River floods, it is still "Multiple dam collapses in the upper reaches" | | This is our magnificent sight!

Kropotkin said: "Today's scientific inventions are very sophisticated, and there is no need to invent any more for the time being. It is enough to have the public enjoy all the inventions that have already been made." So I say: Today, to avoid natural disasters, we must first extinguish human disasters!

Really, friends! We should first extinguish human disasters, and then extinguish this age-old, detestable cry of "Multiple dam collapses in the upper reaches!"

Random Notes on Reading 214

— Little Snow

Lin Gengbai's "Notes on Jielou Poetry" (July 19th Morning Post),

publishes a poem written by Lu Xun in 1931, which was previously published in "Literary News." The poem goes:

Accustomed to long nights surpassing springtime,

A chaste woman with her brood, her temples streaked with gray.

In dreams, vaguely, a loving mother's tears,

On the city walls, the great king's banners shift.

Grieving to see comrades become new ghosts,

Angrily seeking small poems amidst the knife-edged thickets.

Having recited, I lower my head, nowhere to write,

Moonlight like water shines on my dark robes.

Following the poem is a comment from the author of "Notes on Poetry," saying, "The line 'In dreams, vaguely, a loving mother's tears, 'is excellent as poetry, but the consciousness and emotions of our literati class are revealed involuntarily, which is not the case for Bolsheviks." I don't know if Lu Xun was the kind of person Lin Gengbai described, but I cannot agree that such a person would not miss his loving mother. They have blood, flesh, and rich emotions; why wouldn't they miss a loving mother? Without citing far-fetched examples, let's just copy a passage about Kobayashi Takiji from the recent "Literature":

His mother was already old, and he always worried about her. Amidst his busy life, whenever he had the chance, he tried his best to make his mother happy. The older brother (referring to Kobayashi Takiji) was happy when he saw his mother happy.

Mothers are just as lovable in the eyes of revolutionaries! This can also be corroborated by Ding Ling's "Mother" (Literary Series of Liangyou Bookstore, and another short story). I think that Lin Gengbai, in this regard, has either mistakenly believed rumors and "demonized" revolutionaries, or has simply understood revolutionaries mechanistically from the aspect of "iron will."

Zhang Xianzhong in Sichuan 215

— Xu Qinwen

I have five Sichuan friends. One day, we gathered to chat, and the topic happened to turn to our ancestral homes. I learned that none of them were true Sichuanese: Mr. Zhao from Chengdu was originally from Zhejiang, Mr. Wen from Huayang was from Hunan, Mr. Li from Zigong was from Guangdong, Mr. Yu from Neijiang was from Hubei, and Mr. Jin from Emei was from Jiangsu. Their ancestors moved to Sichuan and settled down only about two hundred years ago. They all still retain their inherent regional characteristics, and it is very evident once you mention it. Upon investigation, there are not many true Sichuanese living in Sichuan now; most of them were drawn from various provinces. This is because, at the end of the Ming Dynasty, Zhang Xianzhong killed a great number of people in Sichuan, leading to the saying "Zhang Xianzhong killed all the Sichuanese." Although not all Sichuanese were killed, a considerable number were indeed killed. Sichuan was originally a vast and resource-rich land, so people from various provinces were drawn there.

Indiscriminate killing is common among those who wield weapons. However, the purpose of most people's killings is generally to eliminate dissidents. Zhang Xianzhong's motive for killing was not solely for this purpose. His Seven Kill Stele clearly states: "Heaven creates all things for man, man returns nothing to Heaven, kill, kill, kill, kill, kill, kill, kill!" From these words, it seems that he was killing as a way to avenge Heaven. According to the records in the Book of Shu and the Mirror of Shu, he often threw small children into the air, letting them fall onto the tips of spears, taking pleasure in watching their bloodied and frantic movements and cries. It is evident that his killing, besides being for revenge on behalf of Heaven, also contained a sense of amusement.

It is said that Zhang Xianzhong had many methods of killing for amusement. Once, he had piled up a large heap of women's bound feet and took his favorite concubine to view them. After looking for a while, he felt that the mountain of small feet was missing two outstanding ones to be placed at the top, so he cut off his favorite concubine's feet and put them on top.

Everywhere he went, he would routinely kill a large number of people and then pile up the heads, hands, and feet separately. After counting the number, he would record it in an account and even carve it on a stele.

One night, Zhang Xianzhong killed his own wife and children. The next day, he regretted it. His attendants did not dare to dissuade him, so he killed them all as well. His wife certainly obeyed him, and his attendants were even more absolutely obedient, not daring to dissuade him from killing his own wife. But he killed them all, which shows that his killing was not solely for eliminating dissidents.

Zhang Xianzhong's killing sometimes stemmed simply from curiosity, such as the case of killing a狀元 (the person who comes first in the highest imperial exam). He greatly respected the狀元, but simply because he admired him to the extreme and wanted to understand why he was so talented, he dissected the狀元 alive to see.

Zhang Xianzhong can truly be called courageous in killing, and his methods of killing were also quite diverse. However, he always did it openly and never used assassination methods, which is something we can still admire.

A Dream of the Moon 216

— Sun Yang

Moonlight, like water, pours from the gaps in the window into the dark room, playfully kissing my desk. The desk reflects a dim, gray light, and the still objects in the room take on blurry shadows.

I lean against the desk, quietly gazing at that line of moonlight—gentle, elegant, quiet, and mysterious.

"A dream of the moon!" I sigh softly, patting my chest.

Memories have already drifted far from me, but the remaining traces are enough to stir my heartstrings. I like to recall her—my lover who doesn't love me. I half-open my mouth, silently remembering playful words. The tang of plum juice... Moonlight leaks through the willow leaves, scattering over her and me. The evening breeze of June caresses her hair.

"The moon is for reunions," she raises her head, looking at the sky through the gaps in the leaves with bright eyes.

"We are reunited too!" I squeeze her soft little hand.

"Happiness in a dream, we enjoy it with our eyes open." A sphinx-like smile hangs on her lips as she falls into my arms.

"This is a dream of the moon!" I kiss her lips, like red water chestnuts.

I look at the moonlight and smile proudly. I gently caress my lips, for they have kissed those enchanting lips! The moonlight slowly moves, gradually leaving my desk and kissing the floor. Suddenly, my chest fills with anger, such intense anger that it seems unrestrained by my chest and wants to explode. The lips I kissed are probably kissing another mouth now!

I forget my own body, staring blankly at that line of moonlight.

"A dream of the moon!" I exhale and sigh softly.

Ordinary Matters (23) 217

— Dan Guosun

"'It's really more than twenty li!' said Zhiguang, 'Is that area dangerous?'" "Not dangerous yet," the worker said. "The short devils haven't reached there yet. These past two days, we've been transporting so many things over there at night. It looks like there will be fighting soon."

"'Once the fighting starts,' another worker said, 'it will be dangerous to transport things there. The dangerous place now is still Zhabei, and the most dangerous area is around Baoshan Road to Baziqiao!'"

"'Sanbuzhi is a big array of guns and soldiers,' another worker said, pointing eastward. 'Listen, that array has been making noise for another point-ba-zhong (a period of time)!"

At this point, everyone paused for a moment. Finally, Zhiguang asked:

"Are all the things you're making being carried there by manpower?"

"Almost all of it is being carried," one of the workers said. "We have too few trucks and too many things to transport, so we always prioritize the most important or heaviest things to be transported by truck, and the rest is all carried by manpower, so naturally it's slow!"

"Slow is not good!" another worker said. "When it comes to making things, we can still make it in time, but because we have to carry things, at least one-third of the workers here have to take night shifts to manage the 'carrying' matters, which delays the 'installation' matters! If we add more people to the night shift for 'installation,' then the 'making' people will be fewer, and things will be produced more slowly!"

"We naturally need to find a way to remedy this!" Zhiguang said sincerely.

At this time, Zhiguang had already fallen into a state of deep thought. His near-sighted eyes with deep eyelashes were constantly opening and closing until he finished that lunch.

Then, Zhiguang had a long conversation with these carpenters working at Chenjiabang in a form that resembled both a meeting and an investigation. Finally, he stood up and said to the crowd:

"I greatly admire everyone's enthusiasm for service! I also greatly sympathize with the demands that the workers of Changxing Factory are going to make to the factory! However, in the factory, although I have a kind of power to say a few more words, I can only say it, and I can't just say it and expect people to do it accordingly. Everyone understands this. So now I can only try my best to persuade the factory's owner in the position of a representative! Try my best to persuade the factory's owner! I always want him to be able to implement negotiations!" The crowd applauded, and Zhiguang continued:

"Based on the conversations just now, I also understand the deployment situation of the military authorities. It seems that within a very short period of time, they will build a very solid trench along the thirty-odd li between Zhabei and Wusong. That must be very urgent. Therefore, I understand that the supply of transportation equipment is much more important than other supplies. I am very clear about this, and I will find a way to make the factory owner as clear as I am! Everyone's business, everyone must bear the responsibility, and my heart is on the same line as everyone's!"

These few short and sincere speeches were, of course, very welcome and gave these workers a sense of satisfaction and hope. In their view, the next step was just to find Yao Botang, but Zhiguang also wanted to go to Liujiazhai, so he said to them:

"Now that there's still fighting in the east, how should we go to Liujiazhai at this time?"

"It's hard to say," one of the workers said. "When the fighting was fierce a few days ago, the people of Liujiazhai all moved. That area is too close to Baziqiao! Given the situation today, it seems that it's not necessarily better than that day. It's hard to say if we want to go to that area!"

For a while, it was really difficult to discuss any results, because Zhiguang was determined to go to Liujiazhai to inquire about the soil from Changxing Factory, and the carpenters here advised him not to take too much risk. At this time, the sounds of gunfire in Zhabei had not stopped, and the few airplanes in the air were also circling continuously above the war zone. It wasn't until the leader of the engineering soldiers managing the Chenjiabang area came to inspect at around two o'clock that this small difficulty was resolved.

Grain, Flour, and Wheat Futures Improve 232

Flour: Yesterday, after the market opened in the morning, the flour market for each month showed initial stability. It was rumored that there were many head contracts, and factories were losing too much, so they mostly recovered on their own, thus reversing the trend. Customer trading in longer-term contracts was very thin, with only external speculation continuing to buy, and the amount was not large. Observing the later trend, this month's contracts are bound to be squeezed due to head contracts. As a result, this month's contracts rose by 1 cent compared to the previous day, August's by 0.5 cents, September's by 0.75 cents, October and November's by 0.25 cents, and December's by 0.75 cents.

Wheat: Yesterday, after the wheat market opened in the morning, it generally showed a stable trend. The quoted price for imported wheat fluctuated. Sentiment was in a wait-and-see mode. This month's settlement was also approaching, and receivers other than factories had to settle. Therefore, at the opening, prices fell as low as 3.67 yuan. However, longer-term contracts tended to stabilize due to very few sellers. When the afternoon session opened, sentiment slightly improved. It was rumored that factories would receive 30 to 40 trucks of this month's contracts, and many of the standards were not met. Therefore, sentiment rebounded, and longer-term contracts also rose. As a result, this month's contracts improved by 3 cents, August's by 2 cents, September's by 5 cents, November's by 2 cents, and December's by 3 cents. The spot wheat market remains stable, but there are many medium-quality goods, and high-quality goods are not abundant. Quoted prices: Qintong wheat 3.70 yuan, Yangzhou wheat 3.60 yuan, Jiangyan wheat 3.72 yuan, Xia wheat 3.59 yuan, Xia Xia wheat 3.546 yuan, Gao Xia wheat 3.61 yuan, Xinghua wheat 3.68 yuan, Su Xia wheat 3.80 yuan, Pudong wheat 3.20 yuan, second-grade to 10 cents, boat wheat 3.54 yuan, a total of more than 7,500 bags, which were taken away by Fuxin.

Active Cake Sales, Soybean Market Loosens 233

Yesterday, the sales of bean cakes remained strong. A total of 10,000 pieces of customer cakes and 14,500 pieces of factory cakes were sold. Customer cakes showed stronger rising power, while factory cakes were slightly reduced by 1-2 cents. The soybean market showed a slight loosening in the midst of this active cake sales. Yesterday, Zheng Yangguan soybeans, in addition to 200-300 bags purchased by export brokers at a price of 4.92 yuan, factories purchased 8-9 trucks at prices of 4.88 to 4.885 yuan. Also, Yingzhou soybeans sold 12 trucks at a price of 4.80 yuan, leading to a rebound in market sentiment. However, with the gradual arrival of new soybeans, these old soybeans are bound to be affected.

Grain Market: Coarse Sand White Sugar Stable, Other Sugars Decline Slightly 234

The guild set the initial market price for common grade 24 coarse sand white sugar at 20.15 yuan, later down by 2 cents, setting the zero price at 1.03 yuan, slightly better than the previous day. No. 20 medium sand white sugar was 19.55 yuan, down by 5 cents. Nos. 8 and 9 Dutch red sugar were 16.25 yuan, also down by half a cent. Mark 1 cent. Chao Gang opened a few dozen bags of cotton red sugar at 16.50 yuan.

Zhabei Goods: First Batch of New Hunan Lotus Seeds Arrives 235

The new Hunan lotus seeds market initially saw prices as high as 32 taels per picul. Due to the small quantity, they were all purchased by the Guangdong Gang. Now prices have fallen by 4-5 taels. A small number of Shanghai Gang also brought in some. Yesterday, scattered sales were priced at 72 yuan per picul, barely covering costs. Further declines are expected.

Silk, Tea, and Foreign Firms: Silk Market Lifeless 236

Wuxi's new Changtu silk is transported to Shanghai: Wuxi's spring silk production is abundant and of good quality. Silk factories have been operating for over a month. Yesterday, 56 pieces of new Changtu silk were transported to Shanghai, with excellent body.

Chinese silk shipped to Seattle: The US mail ship Jefferson exported 120 pieces of Chinese silk from various foreign firms to Seattle yesterday.

Rayon sales are in a wait-and-see mode: Rayon sales are sluggish, and the fluctuating exchange rate makes the situation worse. Only the Yanqing Gang purchased 28 cases of Golden Unicorn, Double Liu Hai, and Flying Elephant brands for August delivery, priced from 181.25 yuan to 175.50 yuan net.

Core-Pulled Zhenmei Tea Transactions are Strong 237

Yesterday, due to demand from foreign countries, British firms such as Jardine Matheson and Xiehe aggressively searched for core-pulled Zhenmei tea from Wuyuan, Tunxi, and other areas, resulting in very strong transactions. There seems to be no hope for activity in currently low-quality goods. Both British and Russian firms have considerable intake of Qimen black tea, and Chinese merchants are becoming more assertive, with the market showing a general upward trend.
