Discussions

On the Decline of "Public Morality" and "Human Sentiment" 238

— Huicheng

When one opens the newspaper, one is almost always confronted with news of theft, rape, suicide, and so on. Everyone then sighs about the decline of public morality and human sentiment. Indeed, this is the truth; society is filled with evil. However, we should not be like those Confucian moralists who vaguely and indifferently sigh, for what good does that do? We should calmly analyze the reasons for the decline of "public morality" and "human sentiment" with an objective eye, and ultimately consider how to remedy the situation.

Naturally, people should first fill their stomachs, but the conditions of life are not so simple. In addition to food as the mainstay of life, there are many desires that need to be satisfied. For example, in a certain physiological state, we need sexual intercourse, and at certain times, we also need clothing to keep warm. However, in today's deformed society, can these problems be widely solved? Except for a class of bourgeoisie who can enjoy or exceed these conditions, the remaining people, who outnumber the bourgeoisie, are struggling even with the prerequisite of eating. But humans ultimately have needs. So they rob, steal, and rape. However, some of them feel that these actions are not something they dare or want to do, so they take the path of suicide. In this way, moralists sigh about the decline of public morality and human sentiment.

If we analyze their actions with a logical attitude, whether they are crimes, then we must admit that morally, they are wrong and have committed crimes. But from the starting point of their thinking, they are not only not committing crimes but are also right. Because they are humans! They are animals that should need to eat, wear clothes, and have sexual intercourse!

However, their actions need to be corrected: those who commit suicide should bravely rise up; those who rob, steal, and rape should calm down. Everyone should stand on the same battle line to solve their problems of eating, wearing clothes, and having sexual intercourse. Because doing it alone is easy to run into obstacles.

Am I Really Dominated by the Environment? 239

— Wu Fei

Mr. Li is a graduate of XX University, a man rich in reason. When he first left school life and took a job at a gold exchange, starting to come into contact with society and its ways, he was very conscientious in his work. He was very harmonious with his colleagues. In particular, he was able to be cautious in the disbursement of money and in social interactions. Originally, when he was at school, he heard that a friend had been dismissed for being addicted to gambling, a relative had been dismissed for being infatuated with women, someone had committed suicide due to economic reasons, and someone had an unfortunate incident due to something else. He often wondered, is the temptation of society really so strong? Is the dominance of the environment really so great? So, at the beginning of his employment, he was determined to break through the environment and not be dominated by it. The question of "Am I really dominated by the environment?" was constantly swirling in his mind.

His thinking was too keen. He believed that in the environment of "prostitution, gambling, and smoking," it was easiest to be tempted and dominated. So he had a "four nots" principle: do not enter flower bushes, do not gamble, do not smoke or drink, and do not wear fancy clothes. He was able to work hard to do this, not to be the same as the world. Everyone admired him and gave him the nickname "old beyond his years." But in the gold exchange, all that was present was the stench of gold and the desire for profit. He saw that colleagues who ran side businesses often made a fortune, either earning three thousand or more than ten thousand. His heart could not help but be envious. His eyes could not help but be red. He thought that making a fortune was so easy, so he unconsciously began to act. Then he joined in the operation, hoping to make a fortune. Who knew that his first venture into the world, the first thing he did, happened to be during the world gold tide. The price was falling day by day, and he lost more than a thousand taels. Although he was frustrated, he continued to trade. In less than a week, he lost more than two thousand taels. The amount was large, and it became difficult to cope. Friends and relatives who knew about it advised him not to blindly squander his money in this serious period. He could only wait for an opportunity and not make a futile sacrifice. After listening to them, he suddenly realized. "Am I really dominated by the environment?" He immediately stopped the investment, endured the pain for a while, and continued to practice his four nots principles. One day, someone went to ask him, "Why did you turn back so quickly?" He then gave a speech. "Breaking through the environment is not easy. I don't need to talk about European and American theories. In short, the degradation of virtue and the baseness of personality are the result of being dominated by the environment. For example, very diligent and honest rural girls, after arriving in the city, are imperceptibly influenced and gradually become cunning and fashionable. How many can not be dominated by the environment? Conversely, the ladies and gentlemen of the city, the four major things in life, food, clothing, housing, and transportation, are indeed satisfactory and comfortable. Once they are called to the countryside, they feel uncomfortable living and are unaccustomed to the language.

Page 20

It is boring and very lonely and depressed. How many people can create a new environment? Therefore, in a certain environment, it is not easy to meet the three states of wealth, poverty, and power, which cannot be indulged in, cannot be moved, and cannot be bent. In another environment, such as suffering their minds, laboring their muscles and bones, starving their bodies, emptying their bodies, and disrupting their actions, there are not many who can move their hearts, endure their nature, and increase what they cannot do. Just like I was originally determined not to be dominated by the environment, but I was influenced by invisible temptations and was almost misled. Fortunately, I reined in the horse at the precipice and stopped abruptly. In the end, I was able to maintain myself. Therefore, we must not only not be dominated by the environment, but also break through the environment, and be able to create a new environment for ourselves in order to have a way out." Everyone admired his high opinions and admired him for having his own views.

Modern Celebrity Paintings and Calligraphy - Twenty-One 240

Mr. Zhang Xiaoshi's Painting (Brief Biography)

Zhang Zhaoying, courtesy name Xiaoshi, is a native of Songjiang. He has an elegant personality and a lifelong love of painting. He is also known as the Xiaochi Layman. He is an indoor disciple of Mr. Zhang Shanzi and has deeply inherited the charm of his teacher, thus becoming an expert in painting tigers. The beasts and dragons he paints are powerful and lifelike. Recently, his attainments have become even greater, and his character is noble. The painting on the right is his recent masterpiece. Mr. Zhang is young and strong, and his future achievements are immeasurable.

On "Self-Job Introduction" 241

— Lie Huo

Perhaps it is sympathy for the same illness, or perhaps the problem is too serious. Every morning when I open the newspaper, besides flipping through to see if my article has been published, I stare at the "Self-Job Introduction" people, carefully reading their brief biographies, and carefully pondering the cause and effect of this problem. The result is like a heavy rock, pressing tightly on my heart, suffocating me and preventing me from moving.

This column has been added to this publication for about half a year. The number of people published daily is as many as twenty-one or nineteen, and as few as five or six, averaging ten people per day, totaling 1,800 people. Recently, many newspapers have also set up this column, plus the unrecorded number of people who have not submitted their applications, totaling ten times as many, which is 18,000 people. Although this statistic is not accurate, I think it will only be more, not less. How many people are there in Shanghai? There are already such a huge number of unemployed people, and this problem cannot be considered not serious.

Looking at their backgrounds, most of them are high school graduates, and very few are elementary school graduates. University graduates with bachelor's degrees are next in number, and even some have eaten Western bread abroad for more than ten years.

Looking at their talents and learning, some are proficient in Chinese, some can speak Shanghai, Cantonese, and various local dialects, some can speak, write, and translate English, some are deeply rooted in accounting, and some can draft and draw to serve as engineers.

Looking at their resumes, some have held important positions in party and government agencies, some have worked as employees in foreign firms and companies, some have worked as private secretaries, some have worked as principals or teachers in primary and secondary schools, some have operated their own businesses, and some have worked as managers in other people's companies.

Their backgrounds cannot be said to be humble, their talents and learning cannot be said to be shallow, and their resumes cannot be said to be low. Although not all of them are top-notch talents, at least each of them has a skill. In today's Chinese society, which is in urgent need of talent, they should not be left idle. However, the facts are displayed before our eyes. They are the rejected unemployed.

Why are so many people unemployed? The first reason is the economic downturn, which causes a panic phenomenon of instability in all industries. Therefore, all industries adopt a tightening policy, matters that need to be undertaken are shelved, and those that have been undertaken are reduced in scope. Layoffs and salary cuts are often heard, and therefore, the number of unemployed people in society has increased.

Because of the first reason, of course, the phenomenon of "more people than jobs" is formed. The organs for placing talents are limited, but the people who need to be placed are overcrowded. Therefore, the limited organs are preempted by the following types of people and firmly occupy them.

(1) Those who are good at flattering and boasting

(2) Those who have nepotistic relationships

(3) Those who have a certain background or system

(4) Those who have special talents and learning

This causes the unemployed to be unemployed for a long time. Those who start later leave school and have nothing to do. Therefore, the number of unemployed people is increasing. Under such circumstances, let us look at the further tragic prelude of the unemployed.

Although they are confident in their talents and learning, they see that it is impossible to sell themselves, so they try to suppress their desires and sell themselves at a reduced price. Looking at the prices such as "salary is not counted" and "half-duty," only seeking to provide food and accommodation, it can be seen the intensity of the unemployed's desire for a job. As long as they can barely solve their own lives, they are satisfied. And the eyes for employment are even lower. Those who have been secretaries are willing to be clerks, and those who have been senior staff are willing to be runners. Even high school graduates are willing to be followers. In short, as long as someone accepts them. But unfortunately, where is the response? How many have succeeded?

Since there is no way to go in the city, why not return to the vast countryside? Unfortunately, the countryside is more lifeless and poorer. War, bandits, taxes, natural disasters are urgently destroying it. Can you return? Can you make a living if you return?

These two days, the editor has published a notice saying, "This column has a lot of manuscripts accumulated and will temporarily stop accepting submissions," which makes me suddenly feel that the summer vacation has arrived, and the graduation ceremonies of various schools have been held. It is also said that it is related to "the accumulation of many manuscripts." Graduation is unemployment. This is the conclusion of current education that cannot be concealed.

In this way, at the present stage, the unemployment problem is only getting more urgent. However, "when things reach an extreme, they will turn around."

Perhaps there will be a day of overall solution soon.

Shop Clerk Correspondence

A Painful Plea 242

Mr. Editor:

I have a problem and would be very grateful if you could answer it for me:

Here is a record of my daily life:

I get up at seven o'clock and do the sweeping and wiping until seven thirty. Then the store's side dishes... Then, our manager gets up and immediately takes flour and buys snacks. (Our store is a family business, and the manager's parents and elder siblings live above the store.)

At ten o'clock, we eat porridge. By that time, the porridge and side dishes are all gone, and only plain porridge is left. Whether you eat it or not is up to you. After this task is finished, I do store business. But all I do is move things around and send letters, nothing of any real substance. After lunch, I have to wash the dishes and chopsticks. In the afternoon, it's time for snacks again. Everyone eats different things, so going to one place and then another takes at least two hours. After dinner, in this hot weather, I'm fetching water and carrying bath tubs for people. After ten o'clock, it's snack time again. It's not until twelve o'clock that the day is truly over. Our store subscribes to the Shen Bao newspaper, but the manager has ordered that we are not allowed to read it or any other books. Because when your eyes are on the book, you won't notice if there are thieves outside. Also, after twelve o'clock, we are not allowed to turn on the lights. (Because the manager goes to bed at ten o'clock, and his family doesn't go to bed until twelve o'clock.) After I go to bed, I want to practice and study, but who would dare to violate such an order?

Sir, I am sixteen years old. The capitalist is using these means to make me an incapable person. How will I be able to support myself in the future? This kind of life is truly not a human life! But if I don't like it and go home, that is simply not an option. If I stay here any longer, the years will fly by, and what skills will I have to save my future? Now I have told you my troubles, please answer the following questions:

What methods can be used to make capitalists improve their treatment of employees?

I want to study so that I can support myself. Please tell me where there are free schools. If there are none, please teach me how to study on my own. What methods can I use to escape this kind of environment and find a bright future? I anxiously await your reply.

Answer: The letter describes the painful life of an apprentice, which truly represents the life of apprentices in general stores in China. There are tens of thousands of apprentices in China, and they are all groaning and living under this kind of heavy oppression. However, they can only groan at most, and they will never rise up and resist! The rough-handed and bare-footed workers, when they are truly oppressed beyond endurance, will gather together and shout. They will strike, resist, and their collective passion will erupt like a volcano! They will use their collective blood and collective will to find their path to a bright future. But apprentices will never do this! They will only groan and groan, oppressed to death! This is the fundamental weakness of our apprentice class! Because they do not know how to unite and do not know how to resist, they have been oppressed for who knows how many years, and their lives have not improved at all. Who can be blamed for this? It is all because they themselves are not making progress. I sincerely sympathize with the suffering described in the letter, but I do not have any pity for you. What I want to ask you is: why don't you resist? Are you afraid of hunger, ridicule, insults, and all kinds of oppression? If you have the courage to face the enemy on the battlefield, what are you afraid of?

You asked a few questions, and I will answer them below:

(1) What methods can be used to make capitalists improve their treatment of employees? Forgive my shallow knowledge, but I have never heard of a capitalist who would be willing to improve the treatment of workers! Capitalists are destined to exploit workers in order to get rich, otherwise, they would not be capitalists. There are plenty of ways to improve our own treatment, and that is to rely on our own strength! If you talk about making capitalists improve, that will only happen when all the capitalists are dead, and that hope will never be realized in your lifetime.

(2) Although Shanghai is a metropolis, there are not many free schools. Or, as a step back, you could go to a relatively inexpensive night school. (This newspaper currently has several vocational schools.)

There are schools in the Public and French Concessions, as well as in Zhabei, with courses in English, arithmetic, Chinese, accounting, Japanese, and Russian. The tuition is generally six yuan per semester for beginners and ten yuan for advanced students, which is not expensive. If you are determined to study, you can register at any time. But since the letter says that reading the newspaper is also against the store's rules, then I'm afraid this method of studying may not be feasible either.) For self-study, you can learn what you need. For example, if you want to do business, you must pay attention to ordinary commercial correspondence, calculation methods, and commercial knowledge. In addition, the most important thing is the life experience you gain in your daily life, which is the best kind of knowledge. For example, if you were forced to become an apprentice because you didn't have money to study, and you are suffering all kinds of oppression because you are an apprentice, this is your life experience. You should investigate this: why can't I study? Why do I have to be subjected to the unreasonable oppression of the store manager? Then think about how I can overthrow this oppression? If you can find a way out from this, then your future is truly promising, and it will be much more beneficial than just reading a few dead books! Finally, you ask what methods can be used to escape this kind of environment? In my opinion, based on your abilities and environment, the best thing to do is to go back and discuss it with your parents, clearly demanding to find another job. If your parents do not agree, you should persevere to the end. I think this goal can definitely be achieved.

In short: on the one hand, you should use a spirit of perseverance to seek harmony; on the other hand, you need to move forward with unwavering courage! First, put aside hunger, cold, desires, and everything else, and then you can gain life!

Fiction

Under the Red-Light District (36) 243

— Xilin

(20) I'm not necessarily the only one keeping her company tonight!

Today, Shi Qiao and Wang Hua received two hundred yuan from Chen Tianren. They each took sixty yuan as their share,

and divided the remaining eighty yuan among their accomplices.

Shi Qiao went home, repaid the five yuan he borrowed from Meizi, and paid one month's rent of twenty-eight yuan, leaving twenty yuan for food.

In the evening, he took a bath at the hot spring bathhouse. When he returned home, he had nothing to do. He wanted to talk to Meizi, but it was inconvenient with Livinoff at home. So he thought of the third concubine, but he didn't know if she was at home. He went to knock on her door, and only A Zhen was sitting in the room, thinking about something. He asked:

"Where did Madam Danli go?"

"She went to the Marie Hotel and won't be back tonight," A Zhen said, tilting her head. When Shi Qiao showed a look of surprise, she winked and said, "Doesn't Mr. Li know? I thought you were going to open a room with Mr. Li! Mr. Li, you and our madam are really close!"

"Did she go alone?"

"Oh my, are you jealous of her too? She's also jealous of Mr. Li. Isn't Mr. Li very close to that landlady, that Japanese woman?"

"Nonsense!" Although Li Shi Qiao defended himself, he felt a pang of jealousy in his heart. He knew that he didn't truly love the third concubine, but the third concubine did love him. He felt it was an insult that someone who had loved him was now loving someone else. A Zhen saw this secret and took the opportunity to use her seductive tricks. For example, when she spoke to Li Shi Qiao, she didn't turn her body around, but instead, her buttocks were sticking out towards him, and one side of her face was twisted over her shoulder, with her eyes looking back at him from the corner of her eye. This charming posture was somewhat of an imitation of the third concubine, but when done by A Zhen, a newly ripened fruit, it had a different kind of agitation. She deliberately trembled her voice and said:

"Mr. Li, you're having a lot of peach blossom luck!"

"This thing is half a catty compared to the third concubine! Shi Qiao almost wavered. But A Zhen's posture, which was similar to the third concubine's, reminded him that the third concubine might be making that kind of posture to someone else. So he decisively returned to his room, put on his clothes, and headed for the Marie Hotel.

When he arrived at the Marie Hotel, he didn't know which room she was in. He saw several familiar waiters and didn't want to ask them, so he had to walk out dejectedly. On the road, the traffic of people and cars was still as lively as before the war. Red and green advertising lights, billboards, were still covering the streets, and the prostitutes under the lights were standing in rows, and the business was even more prosperous than before the war. The reason is that the people did not get excited because of the war, but because of the stimulation of the war, they felt that their anger could not be vented, so they turned around and wasted their energy aimlessly! Li Shi Qiao may be one of them... Of course, he couldn't see the phenomenon at the bottom, and he was thinking wholeheartedly about how to do it.

Movie Review

The Republic of China, Year 22, July 26th, Wednesday.

The Silver Screen Replaces the Book 244

— Rui

In modern times, movies have become a necessity for the general public, almost as important as eating, and reading the newspaper every day. However, it is regrettable that this "food" is only limited to the wealthy and the petty bourgeoisie, and that this "food" itself can only provide the audience with "leisure" and cannot provide them with nutrition.

Because of traditional ignorance, ignorance of the people, and cultural backwardness, the majority of the Chinese people lack knowledge. They are almost like starving and withered disaster victims. There are certainly not many such people in the cities, but in the countryside, they make up almost the entire population. How thirsty these people are for the nourishment of knowledge!

Movies are the vanguard of construction and the tool of education, therefore, at this time, they should unreservedly awaken to their great mission. The slogan we are shouting is "The silver screen replaces the book!"

This sentence has already been realized in European countries, especially in the Soviet Union. Anyone who has seen "A New Life" has probably already learned it. That kind of educational method is truly many times greater than the power of books. However, Chinese films have always ignored this point. Recently, the term educational film has gradually come to the attention of Chinese people, and they have realized that building a new China can only start with educational films.

How can the silver screen replace the book? What should be put in educational films? The opinion of Italian film expert Sardi is: "For example, showing major events in various countries, including local events that can be used as a reference,

Folklore and landscape films that show the natural scenery of various countries and the folk customs of the people; vocational training films that show the subjects taught in technical schools; films that show the industry of various countries at home and abroad, such as building railways, building ships, building cars, building roads, building bridges, etc. Secondly, there are health and disease prevention films that show how to prevent and treat infectious diseases. The scope of scientific films is the widest, from the life of insects to crystalline minerals, from plant embryos to the application of light. As for agricultural films, they are even more important. They can be used to promote the best planting methods, so as to harvest abundant crops, and show the continuous progress of farming machinery. As for military films, they are a great help in training new soldiers. So we know that the content contained in educational films is really a lot!

China is in urgent need of this kind of major work, and at the same time, I expect that the emergence of this kind of film will definitely arouse the curious attention and enthusiastic welcome of the vast majority of the people.

Whether it is about the future of the film industry or the education of the people, "the silver screen replaces the book" should give us deep attention. Comrades in the Chinese film industry! How should we work hard to do this step-by-step work of chiseling mountains and opening roads!

Film Reviews

Review of "Eternal Regret" 245

— Mi Wu

Small film companies often cannot compare with large companies in terms of equipment because of economic factors. However, the content of a film will not affect its quality because of the size of the company, so many people are often more tolerant of the products of small companies, which naturally has a considerable reason. However, I personally advocate not letting go of the content of the film. This is my attitude towards criticizing the films of small companies (if it can be said).

"Eternal Regret" is a film that fully believes in the doctrine of retribution. It believes in the cause-and-effect relationship between good and evil and suffering and happiness, and at the same time, it also believes that the law is absolutely correct. Therefore, it not only explains the criminal's actions, which are finally exposed and arrested, but also writes that the criminal escapes in an airplane, but is still shot down and destroyed by the so-called "missile" that was prepared in advance. Isn't this very obvious?

Like other films, the insertion of love in the middle is inevitable. However, this insertion only serves to give the supporters of the law a very satisfactory result, and has no other effect.

We often see old martial arts novels in which the author not only creates a high official to enforce the law, but also creates several "heroes" to help enforce the law. "Eternal Regret" completely contains the meaning of this kind of novel.

Speaking of technology, the director is extremely mediocre. He used the same two flashback shots, which made the audience feel disgusted. The inserted shots were too long, making the audience feel that the development of the story was cut off. The subtitles say that Zhiqi's own invention of the airplane, if it is completely completed, will be one-third faster than ordinary airplanes, but there is no scene of the airplane being completed in the middle, and it takes off. And since it is one-third faster than ordinary airplanes, it is certainly beyond the reach of cars, and on the screen, we see that the airplane has already taken off, and the police call the Public Security Bureau, and then the detective returns home to get the "airplane." After such a long time, the airplane should have disappeared long ago, so why does the airplane fall down immediately when the missile is shot up? Also, since Zhiqi is a long-time bandit, why did he not notice anything when Lilian sneaked into his secret room? And what we see on the screen is that Zhiqi deliberately turns his face away and avoids her, letting her in.

In addition, because there are few interior scenes, the light is generally not very good, and even in the interior scenes, the lighting is too uncoordinated.

In terms of acting, it can be said that no one can perform. The better one is still Wei Guangshou.

Lianhua Establishes Six Factories in Shanghai 246

The films produced by Lianhua have always been praised by the Chinese people. The company has been nurtured by the love and cultivation of the Chinese people, so it is urgently seeking to increase its efforts in terms of quality and quantity. Recently, Mr. Zhu Shilin, the Shanghai branch manager of the company, has seen that society attaches importance to Lianhua films, and that a large number of products are not enough to meet the needs. Therefore, in addition to the original first and second factories in Shanghai, he has set up the Lianhua Sixth Factory (the Lianhua Third Factory is in Hong Kong, the Fourth Factory, but Mr. Du Yu is focusing on researching sound films, and the Fifth Factory is in Peiping, which has been temporarily suspended due to the situation). A preparatory office has been set up in the branch office. On the one hand, he is looking for a suitable location to build a studio, and on the other hand, he is preparing to produce products. On July 22, he hosted a banquet at the New Asia Hotel for the important employees and actors of Lianhua. More than 100 people attended the banquet, which was a grand occasion for a while. At the banquet, Mr. Zhu Shilin announced the purpose of establishing the Sixth Factory, and made a speech on the relationship between films and social education, the importance of Lianhua to the Chinese film industry, and new hopes for colleagues. The speech was very pertinent. Then, the representative of the colleagues made a congratulatory speech, and it was not until about 10 p.m. that the banquet ended with joy.

Lianhua Second Factory Two Fairies 247

Lianhua Second Factory has a night fairy, Cai Chusheng. Although he has recently set his own rules to get rid of nightlife and become a worker under the sun, no matter how he changes, the name of this night fairy cannot be taken off. Recently, in addition to this night fairy, the factory has discovered another fairy, Zheng Jiduo, but this fairy's working hours are exactly the opposite of the night fairy's. He likes to work when the sun has not yet risen. It was found that the first day of filming "The Way Out" was at 4 a.m., the second day was at 5 a.m., and the third... to the present, it has been very early in the morning. According to Director Zheng himself, "The plan for the day lies in the morning, so it is best to work in the most precious morning light of the day!" So, colleagues gave him the name of Morning Fairy. Mr. Zheng Jiduo, the Korean director, laughed when he heard the name.

Zheng Junli "The Way Out" Bleeds 248

Lianhua Second Factory, Director Zheng Jiduo's "The Way Out", the filming speed is very amazing, since the start of filming, it is planned to shoot more than two scenes every day. Director Zheng leads cameraman Qiu Yiwei, stage manager Meng Junmou, Zheng Junli, Tan Ying, Tang Tianxiu, Yuan Congmei, and many temporary actors to shoot inside and outside scenes, which is very busy. In the past few days, the scenes shot are: Penglai Market, the Bund, Nanjing Road Bank Street, pawnshops, and hospitals, department stores. The scenes of Chen Tai's wife's death, pushing the car and colliding with the bus, and being injured by the car after being disappointed in seeking employment, were all shot smoothly. However, when filming the scene where Chen Tai was injured by the car, Director Zheng, in order to be realistic, advocated not using photography skills, but carefully instructed the actors to do their jobs. However, the car drove straight at Zheng Junli, although not at high speed, but the momentum was quite fierce, so Zheng Junli was knocked down, his hands were scratched, and blood was dripping. However, he still endured the pain to complete the performance of the scene before using medicine to bandage it. His spirit of sacrificing for art is really admirable.

Xu Qinfang Complains About Her Big Belly 249

— Set Designer

Xu Qinfang has been having a big belly and raising sons every year since she married Chen Kengran, the former boss of Youlian. As the ancients said, "There are three unfilial acts, and having no descendants is the greatest!" Someone like Chen Kengran, who works so hard at the work of having descendants, may be called a filial son.

The couple joined the Mingxing Company together and cooperated on a "The Road to Fitness," which has not been screened for long. They wanted to make another "Fragrant Grass Beauty," but this star, who is good at having a big belly, is having her belly slightly raised like a small hill again. Chen Kengran had no way to deal with it!

Finally; he thought of a way to invite Xia Peizhen to play the lead in "Fragrant Grass Beauty." Xia Peizhen had just recovered from a new illness! She originally wanted to decline, but she couldn't stand the pleading, so she had to agree, and now she has started working.

It's ridiculous! A few days later, Xu Qinfang said to people, "This time I had a son, I swore I wouldn't have any more. I think; this is just saying it for fun. How can it be done!

"Maternal Light" Plays in Nanjing 251

The Lianhua new film, "Maternal Light", which took half a year to make, will be shown in the Nanjing Grand Theatre in this city, under the extreme eagerness of people in Shanghai. Originally, the film, which was produced by the Lianhua First Factory with all its strength and took half a year, was not intended to be shown in this hot summer weather, but the company authorities recently had to advance the public release due to the urging of public opinion. It is generally expected that when this film is shown, there will be a large audience.

A Tour of European and American Studios (7) 252

— Yunyan

In fact, this is a precarious studio, because the British Lion Film Company can never be as prosperous as President Juarez was in his time. He is a comedian and a filmmaker who is best at making entertaining films. He has made many good films, which have enhanced the reputation of the Pikons studio. Pikons studio is certainly not a luxurious film studio in the UK. It is not built with white marble, but because many of the best British films have been produced in this studio, there is such a place in the minds of a group of people in society.

(9) Elstree (England)

The British International Film Company Studio is in Elstree, England.

In the UK, there is no film center like Hollywood. The places where films are made are scattered around London in a chaotic and disordered manner, but many people generally acknowledge that Elstree (in Herts) is the Hollywood of the UK. There are many studios there, such as Bretner Studios and Royal Studios, but the largest studio in the UK is the British International Studio, opposite Royal Studios. The buildings inside occupy an area of 40 acres. The International Studio was established in 1928. It has nine huge theaters for filming, spread over three huge areas. Two of the theaters are enclosed in corrugated iron houses, which were originally used for shooting silent films. There is also one that is very modern in all its equipment, with three sound stages connected to an impermeable trough in the floor below the water, which is prepared for shooting swimming films. For example, the scenes of the submarine disaster in "Seven Heroes" were shot using this impermeable pipe. Next to these three major studio houses are the splicing room, the laboratory, the car room, and the restaurant, which is one of the best of the British studio restaurants. People from the Royal Studio next door often come to visit. Their dressing rooms are always stocked with countless pounds of snow powder, boxes of powder puffs, and countless gallons of liquid colors. The factory is also very large, with a total of more than 150 carpenters. Every year, it uses 50,000 feet of strips, 10,000 feet of wide boards, and almost half a ton of iron nails a week. The spirit of the material department is very serious. If they are asked to prepare six machine bicycles used by the American police or many Chinese stored eggs within a day, they can do it without hesitation. (To be continued)
